Video Rating: None
Video Description: The International Court of Justice hears arguments about what Israel must do to provide aid to Palestinians in Gaza and the occupied West Bank.

Israel is facing accusations of breaking international law after completely cutting off all supplies to the 2.3 million residents of Gaza in March.
 
Israel says it will not allow the entry of goods and supplies into Gaza until Hamas releases all remaining hostages.

# World Court hears arguments against Israel's Gaza aid blockade | Day two
**Sky News - Israel Palestine:** [April 29, 2025](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk)
*  Good morning. The sitting is now open. The Court meets this morning to hear the following [[00:00:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=0.0s)]
*  participants – South Africa, Algeria, Saudi Arabia, Belgium and Colombia. Each of the [[00:00:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9.68s)]
*  delegations has been allocated 30 minutes for its presentation. The Court will observe [[00:00:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=19.6s)]

*  Dango speaking on behalf of South Africa. Sir, you have the floor. [[00:00:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=34.78s)]
*  Mr. President, members of the Court, it is an honour to appear before this Court on behalf [[00:00:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=55.3s)]
*  of the Republic of South Africa. We appear before the Court pursuant to General Assembly [[00:01:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=60.98s)]
*  Resolution 79-232, which requested an advisory opinion on the obligations of Israel in relation [[00:01:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=66.42s)]
*  to the presence and activities of the United Nations and other international organisations [[00:01:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=75.03999999999999s)]
*  and third states. This resolution was initiated by Norway and supported overwhelmingly by [[00:01:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=81.7s)]
*  member states. We make these submissions while Gaza is once again under a complete siege [[00:01:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=88.34s)]
*  following Israel's breach of the ceasefire brokered by the United States, Qatar and Egypt. [[00:01:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=95.98s)]
*  Israel has also intensified its aggression against Palestinians in the West Bank. Israel [[00:01:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=103.26s)]
*  is blocking food, water and medicines, all of which are essential to life from entering [[00:01:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=108.58s)]
*  Gaza. As cited in this Court yesterday, the United Nations Secretary-General stated that [[00:01:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=115.34s)]
*  Gaza is a killing field. He added, aid has dried up, the floodgates of horror have reopened. [[00:02:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=122.9s)]
*  On 11 April, the UN Office of the High Commissioner for Human Rights reported that Israel, and [[00:02:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=131.3s)]
*  I quote, appears to be inflicting on Palestinians in Gaza conditions of life increasingly incompatible [[00:02:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=137.06s)]
*  with a continued existence as a group in Gaza. Palestinian NGOs and major aid groups have [[00:02:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=144.86s)]
*  warned that Gaza is entering into famine and that in the coming days, the country will [[00:02:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=152.46s)]
*  be in a state of emergency. We wish to emphasise the impunity with which Israel is inflicting [[00:03:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=197.06s)]
*  these harms. Israel continues to act with impunity as it does enjoy some form of exceptionalism [[00:03:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=219.22s)]
*  from accountability to international law and norms. Conversely, any person or entity [[00:03:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=226.66s)]
*  which seeks to hold Israel to account for its inhumane and unlawful actions is subjected [[00:03:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=234.98s)]
*  to countermeasures and censure. The United Nations and this Court has not been spared. [[00:04:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=240.5s)]
*  In this context, the United Nations Relief and Works Agency for Palestinian Refugees, UNRWA, which was established after the 1948 Nakba, is but one of Israel's latest casualties. UNRWA is being attacked in furtherance of Israel's goal to deny the inalienable right of return of Palestinian refugees, the restitution of their land, homes and property appropriated since 1948. [[00:04:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=251.12s)]
*  UNRWA is also deliberately imperiling the existence of Palestinians as a group. [[00:04:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=281.12s)]
*  Mr. President, members of the Court, turning now to the Court's jurisdiction, South Africa considers that the Court's jurisdictional requirements have undoubtedly been met. In relation to judicial propriety, South Africa observes that the Court had in its 19 July 2024 advisory opinion dispensed with the arguments raised by some states in these proceedings. [[00:04:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=293.12s)]
*  The Court held that the arguments did not constitute compelling reasons to decline to give the advisory opinion then. The same reasoning should apply now. In the interest of brevity, South Africa will not repeat the Court's longstanding and clear jurisprudence on this aspect. [[00:05:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=319.12s)]
*  Providing an advisory opinion does not require the Court to prejudge elements relevant to the contentious proceedings in South Africa v. Israel, which South Africa argues, based on facts and law, that Israel is in breach of the Genocide Convention. [[00:05:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=337.12s)]
*  The question asked of the Court in the present matter concerns Israel's obligation as an occupying power and its obligations as a member of the United Nations, and specifically the legal consequences arising from its acts and omissions in these contexts. [[00:05:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=355.12s)]
*  The Court has extensive facts available to it by virtue of the dossier transmitted to it by the United Nations and the submissions made in writing by states. This is despite Israel imposing an information blackout, including through prohibiting the entry of international media and by killing journalists. [[00:06:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=372.12s)]
*  Israel is also denying access to the occupied Palestinian territory to UN agencies, persons and entities mandated by it to investigate Israel's violations of Palestinian rights. [[00:06:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=395.12s)]
*  Accepting Israel's argument under the circumstances that this Court has insufficient facts before it would be rewarding it for its own egregious conduct. Any further actions by Israel that censor remaining humanitarian organizations requiring access, UNRWA in particular, would contribute to rendering Israel's conduct unreviewable. [[00:06:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=408.12s)]
*  The international community cannot accept the reality in which an entire civil population is deliberately starved by Israel, where the United Nations is evicted and deprived of its immunities and privileges, where third states and humanitarian organizations are prevented from rendering humanitarian assistance in solidarity and in fulfillment of their over-harmness obligations. [[00:07:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=432.12s)]
*  Nor can we accept that journalists, aid workers and first responders are being assassinated and then hastily buried in mass graves. [[00:07:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=458.12s)]
*  The United Nations is rightly seized with this matter and calls for the Court's urgent advice on the questions put to it by the General Assembly. [[00:07:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=469.12s)]

*  encompassed with the General Assembly's request is urgently required not just to prevent [[01:12:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4359.84s)]
*  further harming the Palestinian people's right to receive humanitarian development [[01:12:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4365.84s)]
*  support, but also to safeguard the legal foundation in which the UN and other entities conduct [[01:12:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4369.84s)]
*  humanitarian activities. [[01:12:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4378.84s)]
*  Turning to the Court's jurisdiction, our views and the views of almost every other [[01:13:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4383.84s)]
*  state participating in these proceedings are in agreement that, given the legal questions [[01:13:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4389.84s)]
*  raised, the Court has jurisdiction to issue the requested advisory opinion, and that there [[01:13:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4395.84s)]
*  are no compelling reasons for it not to do so. [[01:13:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4402.84s)]
*  On the contrary, given the inhumane conditions to which Israel has subjected to the Palestinian [[01:13:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4407.84s)]
*  people most terrifyingly in the Gaza Strip, we respectfully submit that the Court is under [[01:13:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4413.84s)]
*  a duty to issue its opinion so that Israel's obligation to ensure and facilitate the provision [[01:13:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4421.84s)]
*  of humanitarian assistance by the United Nations, other international organizations, and third [[01:13:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4427.84s)]
*  states are made clear. [[01:13:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4433.84s)]
*  Furthermore, the General Assembly's inquiry into Israel's obligation impacts matters [[01:13:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4436.84s)]
*  of widespread importance, including the operations of the UN and other aid agencies, as well [[01:14:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4441.84s)]
*  as Palestinian rights, a matter of universal concern since the adoption of Resolution 181 [[01:14:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4448.84s)]
*  in the second session in 1947. [[01:14:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4455.84s)]
*  The requests also highlight urgent issues, including Israel's legislative ban on UNRWA, [[01:14:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4459.84s)]
*  military actions, impeding humanitarian aid, and threats to UN privileges and humanity. [[01:14:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4466.84s)]
*  A small minority of a group and states argue that the Court should refrain from issuing [[01:14:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4473.84s)]
*  this advisory opinion because doing so would require it to undertake a significant factual [[01:14:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4480.84s)]
*  investigation which is not appropriate for an advisory opinion, or that the question [[01:14:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4486.84s)]
*  was formulated in a biased manner. [[01:14:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4492.84s)]
*  These arguments, which were rejected by the Court in the Wall and the Israeli policies [[01:14:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4495.84s)]
*  and practices cases, would be similarly dismissed for the same reasons articulated in those [[01:15:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4502.84s)]
*  decisions. [[01:15:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4508.84s)]
*  The same states argue that the Court should decline to give its opinion because it has [[01:15:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4510.84s)]
*  already addressed the subject of the request in its previous advisory opinions related [[01:15:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4517.84s)]
*  to the occupied Palestinian territory, or that rendering the occupied would prejudge [[01:15:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4522.84s)]
*  the ongoing contentious proceedings in South Africa versus Israel. [[01:15:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4528.84s)]
*  These arguments have no merit. [[01:15:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4533.84s)]
*  The present request is self-evidently distinct from the prior requests, as the scope and [[01:15:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4536.84s)]
*  nature of Israel's obligations to ensure and facilitate the provision of humanitarian [[01:15:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4543.84s)]
*  assistance by the UN, other international organizations, and third states was not expressly [[01:15:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4548.84s)]
*  addressed by the Court in either of those advisory opinions, leaving the Court views [[01:15:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4555.84s)]
*  in that regard unknown. [[01:16:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4561.84s)]
*  As for the argument that these advisory proceedings would prejudge the outcome of the Dunecide [[01:16:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4563.84s)]
*  case, that argument fails for obvious reasons. [[01:16:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4569.84s)]
*  As for the argument that these advisory proceedings would prejudge in South Africa versus Israel, [[01:16:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4576.84s)]
*  the Court is called upon to interpret and apply the Dunecide Convention and to determine [[01:16:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4585.84s)]
*  whether Israel's conduct in Gaza engages its international responsibility under that [[01:16:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4592.84s)]
*  Convention. [[01:16:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4597.84s)]
*  To a significant extent, the answer to that question is whether the requisite intent under [[01:16:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4598.84s)]
*  Article 2 of the Convention can be attributed to Israel. [[01:16:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4606.84s)]
*  The answer to the questions raised in these proceedings, which are broadly focused on [[01:16:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4610.84s)]
*  identifying the obligation of Israel to ensure and facilitate humanitarian and other assistance [[01:16:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4616.84s)]
*  throughout the occupied Palestinian territory. [[01:17:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4622.84s)]
*  And do not ask the Court to determine Israel's responsibility under the Dunecide Convention [[01:17:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4627.84s)]
*  and would in no way prejudge that narrow question. [[01:17:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4635.84s)]
*  Turning to the question before the Court, I will highlight only a few key points. [[01:17:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4641.84s)]
*  First, as an occupying power, Israel is bound by international humanitarian law, in particular [[01:17:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4646.84s)]
*  the Hague Regulations of 1907 and the Fourth Geneva Convention. [[01:17:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4655.84s)]
*  Under those norms, and at the bare minimum, Israel must guarantee the basic needs of the [[01:17:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4661.84s)]
*  population in the occupied Palestinian territory at all times, including the provision of food, [[01:17:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4668.84s)]
*  water, shelter and medical supplies. [[01:17:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4675.84s)]
*  It must allow medical personnel to carry out their duties and must not adopt measures [[01:17:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4679.84s)]
*  amounting to collective management. [[01:18:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4685.84s)]
*  But Israel's obligations do not end there. [[01:18:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4688.84s)]
*  Pursuant to Article 59 of the Fourth Geneva Convention, if an occupying power is unwilling [[01:18:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4692.84s)]
*  or unable to fulfill its duty to provide the whole or part of the population of the occupied [[01:18:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4699.84s)]
*  territory with essential supplies and services, as is obviously the case in Gaza, it has an [[01:18:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4705.84s)]
*  absolute duty to facilitate such provision by international organizations or third states. [[01:18:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4713.84s)]
*  These obligations are unconditional and are supplemented by Article 69 of additional [[01:18:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4720.84s)]
*  Protocol 1. [[01:18:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4728.84s)]
*  These obligations are, in the case of Israel, complemented by the duty of raising undersecretary [[01:18:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4729.84s)]
*  council resolutions not to abstract, attack or impede organizations and states from providing [[01:18:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4737.84s)]
*  urgently needed humanitarian development assistance to the population in the occupied Palestinian [[01:19:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4746.84s)]
*  territory. [[01:19:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4752.84s)]
*  As an occupying power, Israel's international human rights law obligations are also engaged. [[01:19:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4754.84s)]
*  Under these obligations, Israel must respect, protect and fulfill the fundamental human [[01:19:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4761.84s)]
*  rights of the Palestinian people in the occupied Palestinian territory. [[01:19:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4769.84s)]
*  These include their right to life, to the highest attainable standard of physical and mental [[01:19:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4774.84s)]
*  health, to an adequate standard of living, to adequate food, clothing, housing, water [[01:19:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4781.84s)]
*  and education. [[01:19:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4789.84s)]
*  The obstruction by Israel of efforts by international organizations, including the United Nations [[01:19:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4791.84s)]
*  or by third states, to provide basic services and assistance to the Palestinian people and [[01:19:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4798.84s)]
*  their occupation in order for them to enjoy such protected human rights entails a clear [[01:20:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4805.84s)]
*  violation of Israel's human rights obligations. [[01:20:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4811.84s)]
*  As a UN member and as a party of the UN Convention on Privileges and Immunities, Israel has further [[01:20:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4815.84s)]
*  obligations relevant to these advisory proceedings. [[01:20:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4824.84s)]
*  Under Article 2, Subsection 2 and 2, Subsection 5 of the UN Charter, Israel must cooperate [[01:20:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4827.84s)]
*  in good faith with the United Nations giving it, quote, every assistance in any action [[01:20:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4836.84s)]
*  taken in accordance with the Charter, end quote. [[01:20:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4844.84s)]
*  Israel's obligation to provide every assistance in good faith to the United Nations encompasses [[01:20:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4848.84s)]
*  the principal UN organs as well as other UN subsidiary organs, including UNRWA. [[01:20:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4856.84s)]
*  As UNRWA's mandate is to provide humanitarian assistance to the Palestinian people, Israel [[01:21:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4863.84s)]
*  duty bound to give every assistance to UNRWA in good faith. [[01:21:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4869.84s)]
*  The attempt by certain states in these proceedings to limit Article 2, Subsection 5, as only [[01:21:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4876.84s)]
*  applying to enforcement action by the Security Council pursuant to Chapter 7 of the Charter [[01:21:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4881.84s)]
*  is incorrect, contrary to this Court's interpretation of that provision in the Liberation's advisory [[01:21:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4887.84s)]
*  opinion. [[01:21:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4895.84s)]
*  Under Article 25 of the Charter, Israel has also agreed to accept and carry out the decisions [[01:21:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4897.84s)]
*  of the Security Council. [[01:21:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4905.84s)]
*  Israel must therefore comply with the Security Council resolution demanding that it give [[01:21:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4907.84s)]
*  unhindered access to those providing humanitarian assistance to the Palestinian people. [[01:21:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4914.84s)]
*  Israel also has a duty to guarantee that the UN enjoys the legal capacity necessary for [[01:22:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4921.84s)]
*  exercise of its functions and fulfillment of its purposes. [[01:22:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4929.84s)]
*  This duty is enshrined in Article 104 of the Charter and Article 1, Section 1 of the Convention [[01:22:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4934.84s)]
*  on Privileges and Immunities. [[01:22:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4942.84s)]
*  Moreover, Israel is under a duty to guarantee the United Nations and its officials the privileges [[01:22:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4944.84s)]
*  and immunities necessary for the fulfillment of their functions. [[01:22:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4952.84s)]
*  The obligation is contained in Article 105, Subsection 1 of the Charter and was further [[01:22:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4958.84s)]
*  developed in the Convention on Privileges and Immunities. [[01:22:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4964.84s)]
*  That Convention provides that the United Nations, as well as its officials, property, and assets, [[01:22:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4968.84s)]
*  are immune from every form of legal process. [[01:22:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4976.84s)]
*  Recently, Israel enacted laws that target UNRWA by revoking its privileges and immunities [[01:23:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4982.84s)]
*  and allowing potential criminal proceedings against UNRWA. [[01:23:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4989.84s)]
*  Officials beat these duties. [[01:23:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4994.84s)]
*  Finally, the Convention states the undisputed principle that the premises of the United [[01:23:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=4997.84s)]
*  Nations shall be inviolable. [[01:23:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5004.84s)]
*  This obligation has several implications. [[01:23:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5007.84s)]
*  First, Israeli authorities may not enter the premises of the United Nations or its [[01:23:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5010.84s)]
*  organs without their consent. [[01:23:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5016.84s)]
*  Second, Israel has a positive duty to protect and safeguard those premises from external [[01:23:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5019.84s)]
*  threats. [[01:23:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5027.84s)]
*  And third, Israel must not attack those premises. [[01:23:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5028.84s)]
*  Importantly, these obligations are not qualified and do not cease to apply in situations of [[01:23:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5032.84s)]
*  armed conflict. [[01:23:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5039.84s)]
*  Thus, Israel's failure to guarantee the inviolability of UN premises can never be justified on grounds [[01:24:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5040.84s)]
*  of military expediency or national security. [[01:24:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5049.84s)]
*  I now turn to Israel's obligation to respect the Palestinian people's established right [[01:24:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5053.84s)]
*  to self-determination. [[01:24:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5058.84s)]
*  I use Coggen's norm, generating obligations ergo ominous. [[01:24:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5060.84s)]
*  If that obligation is to mean anything, it surely requires, at a minimum, that Israel [[01:24:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5064.84s)]
*  allow the provision of humanitarian development assistance to the Palestinian people by those [[01:24:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5072.84s)]
*  prepared to give it so as to strengthen their ability to achieve self-determination. [[01:24:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5078.84s)]
*  Israel's refusal to comply with that imperative while perpetrating unspeakable violence on [[01:24:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5086.84s)]
*  the Palestinian people can only confirm the war's fears about its intentions. [[01:24:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5093.84s)]
*  The Court's voice, confirming the scope and nature of Israel's obligations to ensure [[01:25:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5100.84s)]
*  and facilitate humanitarian development assistance to the Palestinian population, will serve [[01:25:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5106.84s)]
*  as a powerful force in preventing those fears from becoming a reality. [[01:25:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5111.84s)]
*  In closing, the Kingdom of Saudi Arabia wishes to emphasize that the Palestinian people's [[01:25:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5119.84s)]
*  right to self-determination is at the core of the question before the Court. [[01:25:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5127.84s)]
*  The Kingdom takes this opportunity to reaffirm its unconditional commitment to the establishment [[01:25:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5133.84s)]
*  of an independent and sovereign Palestinian state within 1967 borders with East Jerusalem [[01:25:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5140.84s)]
*  as its capital. [[01:25:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5148.84s)]
*  This unwavering position is non-negotiable and is not subject to compromises. [[01:25:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5150.84s)]
*  Mr. President, distinguished members of the Court, thank you for your attention. [[01:25:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=5156.84s)]

*  Mr. President, Honorable Member of the Court, it is a great honour for me to present before you, as an agent of the Kingdom of Belgium, in this procedure concerning the request for consultative opinion submitted to the Court by the United Nations General Assembly in its resolution on December 19, 2020. [[01:45:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6344.84s)]
*  As Belgium has already had the opportunity to underline it, I quote, [[01:46:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6373.84s)]
*  The respect for international law, including humanitarian and human rights, is an angular stone of peace and security. [[01:46:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6380.84s)]
*  The current conflict in Gaza has put international law at risk. [[01:46:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6394.84s)]
*  It is precisely at such occasions that it is essential to reaffirm without any doubt our support for international norms that ensure peaceful coexistence within the international community. [[01:46:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6403.84s)]
*  Regardless of the time it has taken, Belgium will examine certain elements discussed in its written presentation in light of arguments raised by other speakers in the procedure. [[01:47:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6422.84s)]
*  For other aspects of the question, Belgium respectfully refers the Court to the developments contained in its written presentation. [[01:47:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6436.84s)]
*  With your permission, I will first briefly address the question of the exercise of discretionary power in your court. [[01:47:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6445.84s)]
*  Secondly, I will dwell on the obligations of Israel as a member of the United Nations. [[01:47:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6456.84s)]
*  Professor Vajos Koutroulis will then address the obligations of Israel in relation to the supply of humanitarian aid. [[01:47:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6464.84s)]
*  Mr President, to respect international law, it is necessary to know the scope of these rules. [[01:47:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6476.84s)]
*  According to the constant jurisprudence of the Court, when it is called to make a consultation, it should not refuse to respond to the request, except if there are decisive reasons to do so. [[01:48:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6485.84s)]
*  However, no argument that could lead to the Court refusing to give a consultative opinion was invoked in the written presentations of the participants in this procedure. [[01:48:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6502.84s)]
*  In reality, the vast majority of arguments had already been invoked in front of the Court and rejected by them in the context of previous consultative procedures. [[01:48:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6513.84s)]
*  Moreover, if any of the arguments invoked is not a decisive reason for the exercise of discretionary power, it is clear that considering the same arguments cumulatively should not change this conclusion. [[01:48:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6526.84s)]
*  In reality, the present procedure will help the General Assembly to fulfill its role and its functions. [[01:49:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6545.84s)]
*  It is necessary because the two previous consultative opinions, made by your Court and yet in the same general situation, have not been implemented. [[01:49:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6554.84s)]
*  It is therefore difficult, to put it mildly, to see in this new procedure an abusing or abusing of the Court. [[01:49:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6566.84s)]
*  On the contrary, the Court is here to play its role, to say the right thing, so that all parties involved act accordingly. [[01:49:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6578.84s)]
*  Thus, Belgium invites the Court to recognize that there is no decisive reason that would justify not responding to the request for a consultative opinion from the General Assembly. [[01:49:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6591.84s)]
*  I now turn to the second part of my presentation, which deals with the obligations of Israel as a member of the United Nations. [[01:50:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6604.84s)]
*  As a member of the UN, every State assumes certain obligations to the organization, its organs and personnel, in virtue of the UN Charter. [[01:50:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6614.84s)]
*  In addition, other conventions, such as the 1946 Convention on the Privileges and Immunity of the United Nations, take relevant, additional obligations applicable to Israel. [[01:50:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6628.84s)]
*  In this context, respecting international law implies cooperating with the UN and assisting it in its action by avoiding acting unilaterally. [[01:50:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6642.84s)]
*  First, Article 2, paragraph 5 of the Charter predicts that the UN Member States, I quote, [[01:50:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6654.84s)]
*  "...give it full assistance in any action taken by it, in accordance with the provisions of the current Charter." [[01:51:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6662.84s)]
*  As the text of the proposal suggests, this obligation applies to any action undertaken by the UN, i.e. any action of any UN body. [[01:51:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6672.84s)]
*  It is therefore not limited to the decisions of the Security Council adopted in virtue of Chapter 7 of the Charter, [[01:51:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6683.84s)]
*  and also covers the presence and activities of organs such as the Office of Rescue and Labor of the United Nations for the Refugees of Palestine in the Middle East, the UN. [[01:51:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6691.84s)]
*  Obviously, the deployment of the UN and its personnel on the territory of a State requires consent. [[01:51:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6703.84s)]
*  However, this concerns only the territory on which a State exerts its sovereignty. [[01:51:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6711.84s)]
*  As the Court confirmed in the Consultative Life of 19 July 2024, I quote, [[01:52:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6720.84s)]
*  "...Israel does not have the right to sovereignty over some parts of the occupied Palestinian territory and would not be able to exercise sovereign powers over its occupation." [[01:52:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6727.84s)]
*  It is clear that Israel cannot subordinate to its consent the presence and activities of the UN, [[01:52:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6739.84s)]
*  the UN agencies and UN personnel on the occupied Palestinian territory. [[01:52:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6751.84s)]
*  The obligation of cooperation and assistance to any action of the UN can thus be fully implemented in the UN activities, including the UN, in occupied Palestinian territory. [[01:52:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6758.84s)]
*  The measures taken unilaterally in the UN are based in particular on allegations relating to the violation of neutrality by members of its personnel. [[01:52:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6773.84s)]
*  These allegations are extremely serious and must be taken seriously. [[01:53:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6785.84s)]
*  The UN has not remained inactive in the face of these allegations, as other participants in the procedure. [[01:53:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6791.84s)]
*  Belgium underlines the investigations carried out by the Office of Internal Control Services, BSCI, [[01:53:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6799.84s)]
*  which have led to the dismissal of persons against whom there were evidence indicating that they could have been involved in the attacks of October 7, 2023. [[01:53:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6806.84s)]
*  In addition, the UN has asked for an independent evaluation of mechanisms and procedures aimed at ensuring the respect of the principle of neutrality by the UN. [[01:53:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6818.84s)]
*  The report in this context attests, among other things, to the fact that the UN has examined all external allegations of lack of neutrality [[01:53:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6832.84s)]
*  and has opened investigations in the case of Prima Facie, where there was evidence of misconduct. [[01:54:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6843.84s)]
*  In addition, the report indicates that Israel has not provided evidence in support of these allegations, [[01:54:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6851.84s)]
*  according to which a significant number of UN employees are members of terrorist organizations. [[01:54:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6857.84s)]
*  Thus, we are far from the image depicted by Israel within the Security Council, according to which I cite, [[01:54:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6864.84s)]
*  The UN is an essential link of the Hamas terrorist device, which makes the UN itself a terrorist organization, [[01:54:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6873.84s)]
*  and that in Gaza, the Hamas is the UN and the UN is the Hamas. [[01:54:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6881.84s)]
*  Belgium rejects such a qualification and considers that the resolutions of the Security Council relating to terrorism are irrelevant to this advisory opinion. [[01:54:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6889.84s)]
*  In view of what precedes, unilateral actions taken against the UN and more particularly against the UNRWA are not only unjustified, [[01:55:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6902.84s)]
*  but also in violation of the obligations assumed by the United Nations Member States. [[01:55:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6912.84s)]
*  The problems and grievances relating to UN actions must be resolved with the organization and not against it. [[01:55:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6919.84s)]
*  This concludes the second point of the Belgian oral exhibition. [[01:55:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=6932.84s)]

*  Gaza is facing a new risk of famine and malnutrition, [[01:57:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7038.84s)]
*  access to water remains very limited and very unequal, [[01:57:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7046.84s)]
*  and the conditions of suffocation remain alarming and are likely to aggravate the risks for public health. [[01:57:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7052.84s)]
*  It is therefore necessary and urgent to recall the obligations of Israel in relation to the supply of humanitarian aid [[01:57:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7063.84s)]
*  and to clarify the content, keeping in mind that these obligations must be interpreted and applied with good faith. [[01:57:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7073.84s)]
*  First, I will dwell on the content of the obligations of international humanitarian law. [[01:58:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7085.84s)]
*  Second, I will dwell on the absence of reasons that justify the violation of these obligations. [[01:58:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7097.84s)]
*  Mr. President, the obligations of Israel in terms of providing humanitarian aid [[01:58:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7107.84s)]
*  come not only from international humanitarian law, but also from international human rights, [[01:58:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7115.84s)]
*  human rights, the right to self-determination, [[01:58:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7126.84s)]
*  relevant resolutions of the United Nations [[01:58:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7130.84s)]
*  and relevant conservative measures ordered by the Court in the case against South Africa. [[01:58:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7135.84s)]
*  This legal framework imposes on the occupying power obligations both positive and negative. [[01:59:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7142.84s)]
*  In early April 2025, the number of human rights workers killed since October 2023 exceeded [[01:59:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7152.84s)]
*  400. [[01:59:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7165.12s)]
*  Unfortunately, we have no choice but to remind ourselves that it is forbidden to attack [[01:59:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7166.12s)]
*  the human rights of the people of the occupied territory, including all the measures of [[02:00:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7206.84s)]
*  these means. [[02:00:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7218.6s)]
*  When we deprive the civil population of this obligation, Article 59 of the same Convention [[02:00:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7219.6s)]
*  provides that the occupying power will accept the actions of the people and facilitate it [[02:00:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7235.32s)]
*  in all the measures of these means. [[02:00:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7248.08s)]
*  The terms insufficiently provided must be interpreted with good faith in light of the [[02:00:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7251.48s)]
*  other rules of applicable international law, including those of the international law of [[02:01:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7263.5199999999995s)]
*  human rights. [[02:01:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7270.24s)]
*  For example, in virtue of Article 43 of the 1907 Act, the occupying power has the general [[02:01:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7271.24s)]
*  obligation to administer the occupied territories, to ensure, I quote, the order and public life. [[02:01:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7283.88s)]
*  In the articles 11 and 12 of the International Pact on Social and Cultural Economic Rights, [[02:01:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7293.68s)]
*  it is announced that it has the right to water and the right to a sufficient level of life [[02:01:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7303.4400000000005s)]
*  for each person and their family, including sufficient food, clothing and housing. [[02:01:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7311.200000000001s)]
*  The Committee on Social and Cultural Economic Rights explains that the right to sufficient [[02:02:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7320.92s)]
*  food, as stated in Article 11 of the Pact, I quote, must not be interpreted in the narrow [[02:02:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7328.92s)]
*  or restrictive way, from the right to a minimum ration of calories, proteins or other specific [[02:02:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7341.92s)]
*  nutrients. [[02:02:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7349.92s)]
*  The same Committee states that, I quote again, the notion of adequate water supply must be [[02:02:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7350.92s)]
*  interpreted in a way compatible with human dignity, and not in a narrow sense, without [[02:02:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7365.92s)]
*  fully referring to volume criteria. [[02:02:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7374.92s)]
*  It comes from what precedes that the occupying power does not have only an obligation to [[02:02:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7377.92s)]
*  maintain the civilian population alive. [[02:03:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7389.92s)]
*  After all, in occupied territories, the occupier must ensure the order and public life, and [[02:03:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7392.92s)]
*  not simply the life of the civilians. [[02:03:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7399.92s)]
*  Thus, for the civilian population to be considered insufficiently provided, it must not be [[02:03:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7403.92s)]
*  at the mercy of famine or even its threatened survival. [[02:03:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7413.92s)]
*  In this case, there is no doubt that the civilian population in the Gaza Strip is sufficiently [[02:03:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7417.92s)]
*  provided. [[02:03:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7428.92s)]
*  Therefore, Israel must accept and facilitate the actions of its courts, international organizations, [[02:03:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7429.92s)]
*  and state-owned enterprises. [[02:04:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7440.92s)]
*  After this remark on the content of the obligations of the occupying power in humanitarian rights, [[02:04:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7441.92s)]
*  I will focus on the absence of reasons to justify the violation of these obligations. [[02:04:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7452.92s)]
*  This is the last point raised by Belgium. [[02:04:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7458.92s)]
*  Mr. President, respecting the obligations related to the supply of humanitarian milk and [[02:04:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7465.92s)]
*  applying them reasonably implies not seeking to be fined by invoking unjustified international [[02:04:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7475.92s)]
*  rights. [[02:04:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7486.92s)]
*  In this case, these are military and security landings that are put forward to justify [[02:04:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7487.92s)]
*  behaviors that do not comply with the obligations of humanitarian international rights. [[02:04:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7496.92s)]
*  In connection with these justifications, Belgium can insist on three points. [[02:05:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7501.92s)]
*  First, as military and security landings refer to the legitimacy of the use of force, Belgium [[02:05:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7510.92s)]
*  reminds us that such considerations cannot affect the application of the rules of humanitarian [[02:05:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7519.92s)]

*  The article provides that the occupier will take all the measures that depend on him in [[02:06:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7608.92s)]
*  order to restore and ensure, as much as possible, the order and the public life. [[02:06:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7616.92s)]

*  On the contrary, the accent is resolutely placed on the obligation of the occupier to take [[02:07:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7632.92s)]
*  all measures that depend on him in order to restore and ensure, as much as possible, the [[02:07:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7639.92s)]
*  order and the public life. [[02:07:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7644.92s)]
*  The Article 43 of the Treaty of La Haye cannot serve as a foundation for a general excuse [[02:07:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7647.92s)]
*  linked to military needs. [[02:07:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7654.92s)]

*  of Geneva, obligations that are not subordinated to the Article 43 of the Treaty of La Haye. [[02:07:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7663.92s)]
*  Thirdly, the military and security landings are not used as a foundation for a general [[02:07:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7671.92s)]
*  excuse. [[02:08:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7682.92s)]
*  Thirdly, the military and security landings are not mislead by humanitarian rights. [[02:08:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7683.92s)]
*  On the contrary, they are taken into account in all the rules of this right. [[02:08:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7694.92s)]
*  As a result, military landings can only be invoked as the relevant provisions are planned. [[02:08:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7702.92s)]
*  If a rule declares an unconditional obligation, the occupying power will not be able to invoke [[02:08:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7713.92s)]
*  these military landings in order to be not so conformed. [[02:08:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7724.92s)]

*  will not be problematic as long as it remains within the limits provided by the relevant [[02:08:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7737.92s)]
*  rule. [[02:09:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7744.92s)]
*  This interpretation must always be done with good faith. [[02:09:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=7745.92s)]

*  contemporary international law is enshrined in the Charter of the United Nations and is [[02:18:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8320.92s)]

*  is an erga omnes obligation, thus implying that all states have a legal interest in ensuring [[02:19:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8340.92s)]

*  organs. [[02:19:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8368.92s)]
*  With this framework in mind, we turn now to Colombia's second point, namely that of Israel's [[02:19:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8369.92s)]

*  The Republic of Colombia is of the view that Israel, as a member of the United States, [[02:19:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8393.92s)]
*  is subject to two core obligations. [[02:19:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8398.92s)]
*  First, to fulfill in good faith the obligation it has undertaken under and in accordance [[02:20:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8401.92s)]
*  with the Charter of the United Nations, and second, to assist the United Nations in any [[02:20:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8406.92s)]
*  action it takes pursuant to the Charter. [[02:20:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8413.92s)]
*  With regard to the first obligation, Article 2, paragraph 2 of the Charter, require Israel [[02:20:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8416.92s)]
*  to fulfill in good faith the obligations it accepted when it ratified this treaty, which [[02:20:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8422.92s)]
*  in any event prevailed over any other obligation, according to Article 103. [[02:20:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8427.92s)]
*  In line with this general obligation, Section 34 of the General Convention on the Privileges [[02:20:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8433.92s)]
*  and Immunities of the United Nations of 1949 provides that, I quote, when an instrument [[02:20:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8439.92s)]
*  of accession is deposited on behalf of any member, the member will be in a position under [[02:20:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8446.92s)]
*  its own law to give effect to the terms of this convention. [[02:20:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8452.92s)]
*  Therefore, Israel, as a state party to this convention since 1949, is bound by the obligations [[02:20:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8456.92s)]
*  contained during and must fulfill them in good faith with regard to the United Nations, [[02:21:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8464.92s)]
*  including UNRWA, an agency of the organization. [[02:21:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8471.92s)]
*  Regarding the second obligation, Article 2, paragraph 5 of the Charter, which refers to [[02:21:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8474.92s)]
*  the obligation of assistance owed to the organization by all member states, it constitutes [[02:21:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8479.92s)]
*  an essential element to allow the United Nations to fulfill its purposes and principles. [[02:21:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8485.92s)]
*  The terminology employed in this provision is unambiguous and it establishes a broad obligation [[02:21:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8492.92s)]
*  encompassing every assistance in any action undertaken by the United Nations. [[02:21:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8499.92s)]
*  The above extends to agencies and bodies of the organization established under Article 22 [[02:21:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8506.92s)]
*  of the Charter, such as UNRWA, whose mandate is to implement resolutions issued by the [[02:21:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8513.92s)]
*  General Assembly, thus constituting actions taken by the United Nations in accordance [[02:21:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8519.92s)]
*  with the Charter. [[02:22:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8526.92s)]
*  Therefore, Colombia considers that as a member of the United Nations, Israel is required [[02:22:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8528.92s)]
*  to give UNRWA every assistance in any action it takes in accordance with the Charter, including [[02:22:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8533.92s)]
*  by fulfilling its obligations under the General Convention and the exchange of letters in [[02:22:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8539.92s)]
*  relations with UNRWA. [[02:22:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8546.92s)]
*  Colombia shares the view of several states which in their written statements expressed [[02:22:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8549.92s)]
*  that Israel must comply with the obligation encompassed in the condition of its admission [[02:22:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8555.92s)]
*  to membership in the United Nations, as contained in General Assembly Resolution 273 of 1949. [[02:22:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8560.92s)]
*  In this regard, to honor the commitment undertaken upon its admission to the United Nations, [[02:22:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8569.92s)]
*  the State of Israel is obliged to fully and faithfully comply with the provisions of the Charter [[02:22:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8576.92s)]
*  in relation to the presence and activities of the United Nations. [[02:23:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8583.92s)]
*  This entails inter alia bring an end to the occupation, cease all violations of the Palestinian [[02:23:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8588.92s)]
*  people's right to self-determination, uphold the privileges and immunities of United Nations [[02:23:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8595.92s)]
*  property and personnel, refrain from any interference with the delivery of humanitarian assistance, [[02:23:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8600.92s)]
*  whether rendered by UNRWA or other agencies or organizations or third states, and more broadly, [[02:23:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8607.92s)]
*  conduct itself as a peace-loving state in accordance with the principles of international law [[02:23:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8614.92s)]
*  and particularly of international humanitarian law as it will be further elaborated below. [[02:23:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8620.92s)]
*  Ladies and gentlemen, the status of Israel as occupying power over the entire Palestinian [[02:23:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8627.92s)]
*  territory has been confirmed by the Court. [[02:23:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8636.92s)]
*  It has been in effect in this territory since at least 1967. [[02:24:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8640.92s)]
*  As a consequence, Israel has been keen to respect international humanitarian law in force, [[02:24:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8648.92s)]
*  including the 4th Geneva Convention, the Regulation of the Hague of 1907 [[02:24:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8655.92s)]
*  and the relevant international humanitarian law of natural custom. [[02:24:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8662.92s)]
*  The current humanitarian situation makes Israel even more imperial and respected [[02:24:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8668.92s)]
*  and I would like to address the specific obligations that Israel must observe in terms of [[02:24:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8674.92s)]
*  its occupying power in accordance with international humanitarian law, [[02:24:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8681.92s)]
*  in particular in terms of the UN's presence and activities in the occupied Palestinian territories. [[02:24:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8690.92s)]
*  First, as she indicated in her exposition, the Columbia states that the humanitarian aid [[02:24:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8699.92s)]
*  and the basic services to the civil population of the occupied Palestinian territory [[02:25:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8706.92s)]
*  are indispensable to guarantee its protection and subsistence. [[02:25:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8711.92s)]
*  As an occupying power, Israel is responsible for the administration of this territory [[02:25:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8716.92s)]
*  and therefore has the obligation to act in the interests of the civil population that resides there. [[02:25:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8722.92s)]
*  As a consequence, Israel is linked by several rules that exist in humanitarian aid in the context of occupation. [[02:25:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8728.92s)]
*  First, in the context of an international armed conflict, Article 23 of the 4th Geneva Convention [[02:25:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8735.92s)]
*  imposes to Israel the obligation to grant the passage of humanitarian aid to civilians. [[02:25:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8743.92s)]
*  Second, in the context of international customary law, Israel as an occupying power [[02:25:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8751.92s)]
*  must ensure that all the necessary supplies for the survival of the civil population are available. [[02:25:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8759.92s)]
*  In addition, by virtue of Article 59 of the 4th Geneva Convention, [[02:26:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8768.92s)]
*  Israel is entitled to accept in the name of the civil population the actions of aid that could be undertaken [[02:26:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8773.92s)]
*  either by third parties or by humanitarian organizations, [[02:26:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8780.92s)]
*  when the needs of the population are not satisfied. [[02:26:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8784.92s)]
*  The Columbia notes that throughout this procedure, the states have highlighted that Israel's inability [[02:26:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8789.92s)]
*  to respond to the needs of the civil population constitutes a violation of international humanitarian law. [[02:26:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8795.92s)]
*  Likewise, the Columbia supports that Israel cannot simply succumb to its obligation [[02:26:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8802.92s)]
*  to allow the free passage of humanitarian aid based on its own presumptions. [[02:26:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8808.92s)]
*  To be aware of these obligations, Israel must provide concrete evidence [[02:26:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8813.92s)]
*  that the needs of the civil population are sufficiently satisfied. [[02:26:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8819.92s)]
*  The Columbia considers that this is not the case. Israel cannot hide the indispensable resources of UNRWA. [[02:27:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8824.92s)]
*  As a result, the vast majority of participants in this procedure showed that no other organization [[02:27:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8831.92s)]
*  has the infrastructure, the capacity and experience necessary to acquire specific mandates entrusted to UNRWA. [[02:27:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8838.92s)]
*  The Columbia therefore considers that Israel lacks its obligation, [[02:27:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8848.92s)]
*  by virtue of international humanitarian law, to refrain from any action [[02:27:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8852.92s)]
*  by hindering the supply of basic services and humanitarian aid to the Palestinian population. [[02:27:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8856.92s)]
*  Mr. President, Mrs. Chairwoman of the Court, Israel is inclined to refrain from attacking, [[02:27:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8863.92s)]
*  destroying, taking or making the essential goods of the survival of the civil population unusable. [[02:27:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8869.92s)]
*  The Columbia supports that Israel, as an occupying power, must refrain from targeting medical facilities, [[02:27:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8876.92s)]
*  medical staff, emergency vehicles, and must cease to use these medical facilities [[02:28:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8883.92s)]
*  at military expense, according to international humanitarian law in use. [[02:28:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8889.92s)]
*  It must also guarantee that the wounded have quick access to medical staff and ambulances, [[02:28:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8894.92s)]
*  and that they are not exposed to the [[02:28:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8899.92s)]
*  excessive concern of the occupying power and security. [[02:28:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8904.54s)]
*  The international occupation regime has established a delicate balance between humanitarian aid and its concerns, [[02:28:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8914.92s)]
*  namely the control rights stated in articles 23 and 59 and 61 of the Geneva Convention. [[02:28:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8921.92s)]
*  These provisions could not be interpreted as authorizing excessive restrictions [[02:28:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8928.92s)]
*  or generalized based on security motives. [[02:28:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8934.92s)]
*  Those of imperial military needs, with a specific geographical problem, [[02:28:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8938.92s)]
*  can limit humanitarian invoices to a reasonable level. [[02:29:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8944.92s)]
*  As a result, Israel is not entitled to invoke security concerns [[02:29:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8948.92s)]
*  as a general limit to the present and future activities of third parties [[02:29:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8953.92s)]
*  that provide urgent and vital aid to the civil population. [[02:29:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8958.92s)]
*  In the absence of serious and credible reasons, [[02:29:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8962.92s)]
*  the states can also legally prevent or interrupt humanitarian aid [[02:29:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8965.92s)]
*  when the fundamental needs of the civil population are not satisfied. [[02:29:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8970.92s)]
*  If conditions require certain measures to respond to the concern of the occupying power in terms of security, [[02:29:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8974.92s)]
*  they must be treated in accordance with international law and not in the case of national realization. [[02:29:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8982.92s)]
*  As a result of these restrictions justified at the entry of humanitarian aid, [[02:29:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8989.92s)]
*  Colombia considers that Israel is impotent in accessing goods and supplies to Gaza [[02:29:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8993.92s)]
*  by flagrantly violating the prohibition of famine as a method of war, [[02:29:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=8999.92s)]
*  in accordance with the first paragraph of article 54 of the first additional protocol and article 14 of the second additional protocol. [[02:30:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9003.92s)]

*  in the South African affair of Israel on January 26, 2024, in which it asked Israel to take, I quote, [[02:30:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9029.92s)]
*  all the measures in their power to prevent the commission of all the relevant acts of article 2 of the Convention on Genocide of 1948. [[02:30:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9037.92s)]
*  Mr. President, in accordance with the UN principles, [[02:30:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9047.92s)]
*  this has always implemented an essential mandate in the occupied Palestinian territories. [[02:30:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9051.92s)]

*  and the refusal of registration by UNRWA. [[02:31:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9063.92s)]
*  Colombia shares the view expressed in several written exposés, [[02:31:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9067.92s)]

*  The State of Israel therefore lacks openly the obligations that accompany it [[02:32:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9125.92s)]

*  Mr. President, the Court has a well-established tradition of addressing the consequences of the facts [[02:32:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9150.92s)]

*  Mr. President, Madam and Mr. Speaker, and even the Court, to conclude, I respectfully [[02:34:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9296.92s)]

*  the fundamental principles and obligations consecrated by the international humanitarian [[02:35:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9341.92s)]
*  aid, in particular those that compromise the occupying power during the occupation in [[02:35:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9346.92s)]
*  the best interests of all the protected persons who are placed under its effective control. [[02:35:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9351.92s)]
*  Colombia also considers that by arbitrarily refusing to give its consent to the UN to [[02:35:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9357.92s)]
*  pursue these operations and to intervene in the work of other international organizations [[02:36:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9362.92s)]
*  in the Palestinian occupied territories, Israel condemns the population of Gaza to an [[02:36:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9368.92s)]
*  aggravation of the humanitarian crisis. [[02:36:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9374.92s)]

*  in circumstances such as those to which Palestinian refugees are confronted, such a refusal [[02:36:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9382.92s)]

*  ... as intransgressible principles. [[02:38:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9534.92s)]
*  These include absolute prohibitions on their international humanitarian law against collective [[02:38:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9537.92s)]
*  punishment, deliberate starvation, attacks on objects indispensable to survival and respect [[02:39:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9542.92s)]
*  for non-derogable human rights. [[02:39:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9548.92s)]
*  Widespread denial of essential aid amounts to a breach of these fundamental rules. [[02:39:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9550.92s)]
*  Second, even where international humanitarian law permits security exceptions, these exceptions [[02:39:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9556.92s)]
*  are narrowly defined and strictly conditioned. [[02:39:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9562.92s)]
*  The obligation under Article 59 of the Four Geneva Convention to agree to and facilitate relief [[02:39:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9566.92s)]
*  contains no explicit security exception, allowing refusal or systematic obstruction of relief schemes [[02:39:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9572.92s)]
*  undertaken by states or impartial organizations. [[02:39:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9580.92s)]
*  In any event, its requirements relating to population under occupation are distinct from the limited [[02:39:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9584.92s)]
*  ability of a state to control access to third-party aid within its territory. [[02:39:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9591.92s)]
*  Third, Israel's security concerns cannot displace the specific and generally absolute nature of the [[02:39:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9598.92s)]
*  privileges and immunities of the UN. [[02:40:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9606.92s)]
*  UNDRA, as a UN organ, benefits from these protections under the Charter and the General Convention. [[02:40:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9608.92s)]
*  Article 105 of the Charter obliges all members to grant the organization and its officials the privileges [[02:40:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9615.92s)]
*  and immunities necessary for the fulfillment of its purposes and necessary for the independent [[02:40:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9622.92s)]
*  exercise of their functions. [[02:40:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9628.92s)]
*  The General Convention implements this Charter duty without replacing it or superseding it. [[02:40:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9631.92s)]
*  These protections cannot be overridden by any security exceptions stemming from international [[02:40:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9638.92s)]
*  humanitarian law. [[02:40:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9644.92s)]
*  Specifically, the inviolability of UN premises under Article 2, Section 3 of the General Convention [[02:40:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9646.92s)]
*  is absolute. [[02:40:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9652.92s)]
*  It admits no exception, whether because of alleged misuse or security concerns asserted unilaterally [[02:40:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9654.92s)]
*  by the occupying power or any other basis. [[02:41:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9662.92s)]
*  As to the functional immunities of UN personnel, Israel cannot unilaterally decide whether specific [[02:41:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9667.92s)]
*  conduct falls outside of the official function. [[02:41:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9674.92s)]
*  That determination lies within the Secretary General or his delegate, UNDRA's Commissioner General. [[02:41:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9678.92s)]
*  And concerns about individuals must be addressed through established UN channels, including, [[02:41:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9685.92s)]
*  where appropriate, through seeking a waiver. [[02:41:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9691.92s)]
*  Finally, even if security measures were permitted, they would have to be applied in good faith, [[02:41:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9694.92s)]
*  consistent with Article 2, Paragraph 2 of the Charter and customary international law. [[02:41:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9702.92s)]

*  As the Court held in its 2024 advisory opinion, [[02:42:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9750.92s)]
*  Israel's presence in the Palestinian Gaza Strip and West Bank, including East Jerusalem, is, in and of itself, illegal. [[02:42:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9755.92s)]
*  It's a violation of the legal right of self-determination of the Palestinian people. [[02:42:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9766.92s)]
*  It's conducted for the unlawful purpose of purported annexation. [[02:42:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9772.92s)]
*  It must, in the words of the Court, end as rapidly as possible. [[02:42:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9778.92s)]
*  These findings presuppose that Israel has no valid legal basis to maintain the presence. [[02:43:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9785.92s)]
*  Had there been a valid legal basis, the Court would not have called for the presence to end. [[02:43:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9794.92s)]
*  The Court characterised the presence as a use of force, [[02:43:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9803.92s)]
*  the legality of which determined by the law of the use of force. [[02:43:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9808.92s)]
*  Since using force without a valid legal basis is a breach of the yos ad bellam, [[02:43:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9813.92s)]
*  the implication of the Court's finding that the presence should end [[02:43:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9821.92s)]
*  is that the presence is an unlawful use of force, an aggression. [[02:43:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9827.92s)]
*  Only the state of Palestine and the Palestinian people have the legal right to exercise authority in the Gaza Strip and West Bank, including East Jerusalem. [[02:43:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9834.92s)]
*  In consequence, only they have the legal right to decide who can enter and be present there [[02:44:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9847.92s)]
*  and which activities those present can engage in. [[02:44:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9855.92s)]
*  Conversely, as its presence is illegal, Israel necessarily lacks a valid entitlement to do anything there. [[02:44:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9860.92s)]
*  Insofar then, as the presence continues, every activity performed is itself illegal, as an integral part of an illegal presence. [[02:44:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9872.92s)]
*  In consequence, Israel has no legal right to take any action in the OPT, [[02:44:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9887.92s)]
*  restricting the entry, presence and activities of other actors. [[02:44:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9895.92s)]
*  Any such action, on whatever basis, is therefore illegal. [[02:45:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9901.92s)]
*  That said, in particular circumstances, the rules regulating the conduct of the Israeli presence, including occupation law, [[02:45:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9909.92s)]
*  don't prevent and even permit and require certain restrictions on the entry, presence and activities of other actors. [[02:45:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9920.92s)]
*  Given this, it might be suggested that international law creates a paradoxical, perverse situation. [[02:45:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9932.92s)]
*  On the one hand, as the court determined, the presence is unlawful and should therefore end as rapidly as possible. [[02:45:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9942.92s)]
*  On the other hand, because Israel defies the court and continues its illegal presence, [[02:45:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9953.92s)]
*  obligations are then triggered, permitting it to decide on the presence of other actors, [[02:46:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9961.92s)]
*  and do so against the wishes of the only legal persons entitled to do this. [[02:46:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9969.92s)]
*  This suggestion would be to misunderstand the relative significance of the two areas of law. [[02:46:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9978.92s)]
*  As the court held, the legal rules governing the conduct of the presence apply even though the presence is illegal. [[02:46:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9987.92s)]
*  However, because of that illegality, all Israel's actions performed as part of the presence will be illegal on this basis, [[02:46:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=9998.92s)]
*  including actions compliant with and pursuant to the rules regulating conduct. [[02:46:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10009.92s)]
*  Thus, ultimately, restrictions that are lawful according to the rules regulating conduct remain unlawful [[02:46:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10018.92s)]
*  according to the law of self-determination and the yos ad belim, [[02:47:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10029.92s)]
*  since they are performed as part of a presence that is, as a general, unqualified matter, illegal. [[02:47:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10034.92s)]
*  On this basis, Israeli restrictions in the OPT on the entry, presence and activities of other actors [[02:47:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10044.92s)]
*  are breaches of Israel's obligations owed to the Palestinian people and the state of Palestine. [[02:47:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10053.92s)]
*  Moreover, such restrictions are also violations of other obligations Israel owes to states. [[02:47:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10060.92s)]
*  Many states are present in the OPT on a profoundly different basis than Israel, [[02:47:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10071.92s)]

*  As the court held, because of the fundamental nature of the Palestinian right of self-determination [[02:48:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10101.92s)]
