*  Providing assistance reduces the dependency of the Palestinian people on the state [[02:49:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10158.92s)]
*  perpetuating its subjugation of them through its presence. [[02:49:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10165.92s)]
*  Israeli restrictions conducted in the OPT to the entry, presence and activities of states [[02:49:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10172.92s)]

*  impede their ability to perform activities benefiting the Palestinian people. [[02:49:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10195.92s)]
*  As a result, they constitute an unlawful interference by Israel [[02:50:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10202.92s)]
*  in these states' ability to discharge that special legal duty owed to the Palestinian people. [[02:50:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10208.92s)]

*  that Israel's presence in the OPT is, in and of itself, illegal is as follows. [[02:50:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10222.92s)]

*  Any such action is illegal. [[02:50:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10246.92s)]

*  requested this Court to render an advisory opinion on Israel's obligations regarding the presence [[02:54:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10442.92s)]
*  and activities of the United Nations, other international organizations, and third party states [[02:54:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10448.92s)]
*  in and in relation to the occupied Palestinian territory. [[02:54:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10455.92s)]
*  Brazil, alongside 52 other countries, co-sponsored the Resolution and submitted a written statement [[02:54:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10461.92s)]
*  to the Court on the 28th of February, grounding our stance in our unwavering commitment [[02:54:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10469.92s)]
*  to promoting international law and recognizing the crucial role of the International Court of Justice [[02:54:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10476.92s)]
*  in fostering justice and peace. [[02:54:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10482.92s)]
*  In the first phase of the proceedings, over 40 countries and international organizations [[02:54:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10487.92s)]
*  chose to participate and furnish elements to support the Court's deliberation. [[02:54:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10492.92s)]
*  The widespread engagement highlights not only the importance of the matter at hand, [[02:54:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10497.92s)]
*  but also the grave concern that Israel's actions in Palestine, not only in Gaza, but also in the West Bank, [[02:55:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10502.92s)]
*  including East Jerusalem, have sparked within the international community. [[02:55:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10509.92s)]
*  The ongoing catastrophe in Gaza, now reaching 18 months, has already claimed over 51,000 lives, [[02:55:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10516.92s)]
*  most of whom women and children. [[02:55:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10524.92s)]
*  After a brief ceasefire, during which hostages were released and desperately needed humanitarian aid, [[02:55:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10526.92s)]
*  was temporarily allowed to reach the population of Gaza, [[02:55:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10533.92s)]
*  Israel resumed blocking food, medicine, and other essential supplies from entering the territory, [[02:55:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10537.92s)]
*  restarted its attacks, and launched a new ground offensive in Gaza. [[02:55:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10543.92s)]
*  In this troubling context, the present advisory opinion is sorely and urgently needed. [[02:55:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10548.92s)]
*  Mr. President, the written statement submitted by Brazil expresses the view that the Court has jurisdiction [[02:55:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10556.92s)]
*  to issue the requested advisory opinion in accordance with Article 65.1 of its statute. [[02:56:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10564.92s)]
*  There is, therefore, no reason for the Court to refrain from issuing the requested advisory opinion. [[02:56:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10572.92s)]
*  The issue before the Court does not constitute a bilateral dispute that would warrant the non-exercise of its jurisdiction. [[02:56:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10578.92s)]
*  On the contrary, it concerns legal obligations in a general sense, [[02:56:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10586.92s)]
*  within the scope of multilateral agreements and treaties, which must be complied with and respected. [[02:56:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10591.92s)]
*  Distinguished judges, the right of the Palestinian people to self-determination has already been recognized by this Court. [[02:56:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10598.92s)]
*  Self-determination is one of the essential principles of international law, [[02:56:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10607.92s)]
*  explicitly enshrined in the United Nations Charter and considered by the General Assembly [[02:56:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10612.92s)]
*  as an inseparable element of fundamental human rights. [[02:56:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10618.92s)]
*  As stated by the Court, self-determination entails, among other elements, [[02:57:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10622.92s)]
*  the right to territorial integrity and the right to freely determine its political status [[02:57:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10628.92s)]
*  and to pursue its economic, social, and cultural development. [[02:57:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10634.92s)]
*  Indeed, the General Assembly has repeatedly affirmed the Palestinian people's right to self-determination, [[02:57:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10638.92s)]
*  including the right to an independent and sovereign state of Palestine. [[02:57:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10646.92s)]
*  Other United Nations bodies, such as the Human Rights Council, have done the same. [[02:57:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10650.92s)]
*  In its advisory opinion on the legal consequences of Israel's practices and policies in the occupied Palestinian territory, [[02:57:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10655.92s)]
*  including East Jerusalem, this Court stated that Israel, as the occupying power, [[02:57:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10663.92s)]
*  has the obligation not to impede the Palestinian people from exercising its right to self-determination, [[02:57:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10670.92s)]
*  including its right to an independent and sovereign state over the entirety of the occupied Palestinian territory. [[02:57:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10677.92s)]
*  In this regard, Brazil contends and hopes that the Court will acknowledge that all the measures [[02:58:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10685.92s)]
*  systematically adopted by Israel to impede or hinder the presence and activities of the United Nations, [[02:58:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10694.92s)]
*  other international organizations, and third-party states in the occupied Palestinian territory [[02:58:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10700.92s)]
*  blatantly violate not only the Palestinian right to self-determination, [[02:58:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10706.92s)]
*  but also other fundamental obligations under general international law. [[02:58:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10711.92s)]
*  Mr. President, the United Nations Relief and Works Agency for Palestine Refugees in the Near East, UNRWA, [[02:58:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10716.92s)]
*  was established by the General Assembly in 1949 to provide assistance to Palestinian refugees. [[02:58:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10726.92s)]
*  Only the General Assembly has the authority to review or revoke its mandate, [[02:58:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10733.92s)]
*  which cannot be subjected to restrictions imposed by any domestic legislation. [[02:58:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10738.92s)]
*  UNRWA is the backbone of the United Nations humanitarian operations in favor of Palestinian refugees [[02:59:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10744.92s)]
*  providing education, health care, social services, and emergency assistance. [[02:59:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10751.92s)]
*  It provides aid for over 6 million people. [[02:59:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10758.92s)]
*  Its presence and work are even more urgent in the current context of near-total destruction in Gaza, [[02:59:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10761.92s)]
*  where it serves over 2 million people. [[02:59:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10767.92s)]
*  In 2024, contrary to international law, Israel passed two bills aimed at severely hindering UNRWA's operations [[02:59:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10771.92s)]
*  within the occupied Palestinian territory, including East Jerusalem. [[02:59:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10780.92s)]
*  At the time, Brazil immediately expressed its grave concern regarding this measure. [[02:59:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10785.92s)]
*  We emphasized that it constitutes a blatant violation of international law [[02:59:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10791.92s)]
*  in direct opposition to binding decisions of this court related to the occupying power's obligation [[02:59:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10796.92s)]
*  to ensure humanitarian access to the citizens of the occupied Palestinian territory. [[03:00:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10804.92s)]
*  As a member of UNRWA's advisory commission, in which it currently holds one of the two vice-presidencies, [[03:00:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10810.92s)]
*  Brazil urged the Israeli government to refrain from implementing these provisions [[03:00:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10818.92s)]
*  in order to allow UNRWA's work to continue in all the occupied Palestinian territory. [[03:00:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10823.92s)]
*  We regret that Israel has not revisited this measure, [[03:00:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10829.92s)]
*  having instead undertaken measures to prevent UNRWA from carrying out its activities, especially in East Jerusalem. [[03:00:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10835.92s)]
*  And we hope that this court will declare the absolute illegality of these actions. [[03:00:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10842.92s)]
*  There is no realistic alternative to UNRWA in providing services and assistance to the Palestinian refugees. [[03:00:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10848.92s)]
*  Any attempt to obstruct UNRWA's operations, whether through legislative, financial, or physical barriers, [[03:00:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10855.92s)]
*  does not alter the established rights of Palestinian refugees. [[03:01:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10863.92s)]
*  Hindering or undermining the ability of UNRWA to fulfill its mandate [[03:01:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10868.92s)]
*  does not alter the established legal protections afforded to Palestinian refugees. [[03:01:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10873.92s)]
*  Both as the occupying power, as well as a member of the United Nations, [[03:01:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10879.92s)]
*  Israel is obligated to facilitate and enable UNRWA's operations in the occupied Palestinian territory. [[03:01:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10886.92s)]
*  It cannot interfere with or obstruct the exercise of this mandate, which was established by the General Assembly. [[03:01:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10893.92s)]
*  Distinguished judges, I will now make specific remarks regarding Israel's obligations as an occupying power. [[03:01:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10901.92s)]
*  In its wall advisory opinion, the court confirmed that the Fourth Geneva Convention applies to any territory occupied [[03:01:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10911.92s)]
*  following an armed conflict between high contracting parties. [[03:02:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10920.92s)]
*  Israel and Jordan were both parties to the Convention when the 1967 conflict broke out. [[03:02:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10924.92s)]
*  Therefore, the court found that the Convention applies to the Palestinian territory occupied by Israel since that time. [[03:02:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10933.92s)]
*  This position had already been asserted by the Security Council in Resolutions 636 and 641. [[03:02:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10941.92s)]
*  In its 2024 advisory opinion, the court reaffirmed that the occupied Palestinian territory is a single territorial unit [[03:02:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10949.92s)]
*  and that Gaza remains an integral part of the area occupied by Israel in 1967. [[03:02:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10959.92s)]
*  Although Israel had withdrawn its military presence from Gaza in 2005, [[03:02:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10965.92s)]
*  it continued to exercise control over the territory in key ways, [[03:02:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10971.92s)]
*  including through restrictions on movement, border control, taxation, and military operations in the buffer zone. [[03:02:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10976.92s)]
*  This control has terrifyingly evolved since October 2023. [[03:03:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10984.92s)]
*  As an occupying power, Israel has legal obligations under the law of occupation. [[03:03:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10990.92s)]
*  The occupying power must administer the territory for the benefit of the local population while refraining from any acts of sovereignty. [[03:03:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=10997.92s)]
*  The obligations of an occupying power are clearly outlined in the relevant conventions [[03:03:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11007.92s)]
*  and consistently restated in this court's opinions and in permanent resolutions of the United Nations General Assembly and Security Council. [[03:03:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11013.92s)]
*  Israel must guarantee public order and safety while respecting local laws. [[03:03:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11023.92s)]
*  It must also ensure access to essential services, including education, medical care, food, and humanitarian aid. [[03:03:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11030.92s)]
*  Any failure to meet these obligations constitutes a blatant violation of international law. [[03:03:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11039.92s)]
*  In other words, the international obligation to protect the civilian population is not limited to the duty of refraining from attacking civilians [[03:04:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11046.92s)]
*  or international organizations or third states providing humanitarian assistance. [[03:04:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11056.92s)]
*  In fact, it embodies the obligation to respect and ensure respect, [[03:04:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11061.92s)]
*  which in any unbiased view also entails the positive duty to facilitate such assistance as provided for, [[03:04:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11068.92s)]
*  for example, in Security Council Resolution 2720 of 2023, [[03:04:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11077.92s)]
*  which demands the facilitation and enablement of the immediate, safe, and unhindered delivery of humanitarian assistance. [[03:04:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11083.92s)]
*  In the proceedings instituted by South Africa against Israel concerning the application of the Convention on the Prevention and Punishment of the Crime of Genocide in the Gaza Strip, [[03:04:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11092.92s)]
*  this court issued on 26 January 2024 provisional measures ordering Israel to allow the urgent provision of humanitarian aid. [[03:05:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11104.92s)]
*  On 28 March 2024, the court reinforced this obligation ordering Israel to ensure the delivery of food, water, fuel, electricity, medical supplies, and shelter in full cooperation with the United Nations. [[03:05:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11115.92s)]
*  Furthermore, the court ruled that Israel's military must not obstruct humanitarian assistance or commit acts that violate the rights of Palestinians in Gaza under the Genocide Convention. [[03:05:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11132.92s)]
*  Under Article 94 of the UN Charter, these measures are binding. [[03:05:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11145.92s)]
*  Beyond legal restrictions, physical barriers to humanitarian assistance such as border closures, travel restrictions, and denial of reentry are also unacceptable. [[03:05:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11152.92s)]
*  These actions only deepen the suffering of the Palestinian people. [[03:06:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11164.92s)]
*  Israel cannot prohibit, restrict, or hinder the United Nations, other international organizations, or third states from providing humanitarian assistance in the occupied Palestinian territory. [[03:06:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11169.92s)]
*  The situation in the occupied Palestinian territory is not only a humanitarian tragedy and a political disaster, but it also entails serious breaches of preemptory norms of international law. [[03:06:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11185.92s)]
*  The principles at stake, self-determination, the prohibition of annexation, and the protection of civilians under occupation, are at the core of international law. [[03:06:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11200.92s)]
*  Compliance with the Fourth Geneva Convention and the rulings of this court is not optional. It is a legal imperative. [[03:06:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11214.92s)]
*  Under these conditions, Israel cannot invoke domestic law to exempt itself from the responsibility arising from these obligations. [[03:07:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11224.92s)]
*  In line with what this court affirmed in its 1996 advisory opinion on the legality of the threat of use of nuclear weapons, paragraph 79, and I quote, [[03:07:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11233.92s)]
*  A great many rules of humanitarian law applicable in armed conflict are so fundamental to the respect of the human person and elementary considerations as humanity, [[03:07:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11246.92s)]
*  as the court put it in its judgment of 9 April 1949 in the Corfu Channel case, that the Hague and Geneva Conventions have enjoyed a broad accession. [[03:07:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11258.92s)]
*  Further, these fundamental rules are to be observed by all states, whether or not they have ratified the conventions that contain them, because they constitute intransgressible principles of international customary law. End of quote. [[03:07:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11270.92s)]
*  Mr. President, Brazil also wishes to highlight Israel's obligations not only as an occupying power and under the international humanitarian law, but also as a member of the United Nations. [[03:08:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11287.92s)]
*  This encompasses obligations concerning the privileges and immunities of the United Nations and its agencies, particularly UNRWA. [[03:08:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11300.92s)]
*  The UN Charter in Article 2, paragraph 3, established that all member states must fulfill their obligations in good faith. [[03:08:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11309.92s)]
*  Additionally, Article 2, paragraph 5, mandates that all states provide the United Nations with every assistance necessary for the implementation of its actions. [[03:08:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11318.92s)]
*  Consequently, Israel is legally required to facilitate UNRWA's operations in accordance with the relevant decisions of competent UNRWA organs, including the General Assembly Resolution 302 and subsequent resolutions that have consistently renewed UNRWA's mandate. [[03:08:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11331.92s)]
*  Furthermore, all UN member states must respect the privileges and immunities granted to the organization, its subsidiary bodies, and specialized agencies. [[03:09:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11352.92s)]
*  Article 105 of the Charter affirms that the United Nations shall enjoy, in the territory of each member, the privileges and immunities necessary for the fulfillment of its purposes. [[03:09:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11364.92s)]
*  This protection extends to representatives of member states and officials of the organization, ensuring their ability to exercise their functions independently. [[03:09:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11378.92s)]
*  Since 1949, Israel has been a party to the Convention on the Privileges and Immunities of the United Nations, the General Convention, which applies to UNRWA as a subsidiary body of the General Assembly and therefore an integral part of the UN system. [[03:09:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11392.92s)]
*  The General Convention clearly stipulates, in Section 3, that UN premises are inviolable and that UN property and assets, regardless of location, are immune from search, requisition, confiscation, expropriation, and any other form of interference, whether by executive, administrative, judicial, or legislative action. [[03:10:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11411.92s)]
*  Additionally, the organization and its property are exempt from all direct taxes under Section 7. [[03:10:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11435.92s)]
*  United Nations officials also benefit from specific protections under Section 18 of the General Convention, including immunity from legal proceedings regarding acts performed in their official capacity, exemption from taxation on their salaries, and immunity from national service obligations. [[03:10:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11442.92s)]
*  These officials, along with their families, are protected from immigration restrictions and granted privileges like those enjoyed by diplomatic personnel. [[03:11:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11460.92s)]
*  Experts on UN missions are also granted necessary immunities to ensure the independent exercise of their functions, including immunity from arrest, detention, and legal proceedings, as established in Section 22. [[03:11:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11469.92s)]
*  Additionally, the General Convention mandates that the United Nations laissez-passer be recognized as a valid travel document by all member states, and that visa applications from UN personnel traveling for official business be processed expeditiously, Section 25. [[03:11:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11484.92s)]
*  Israel has long recognized these obligations. [[03:11:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11505.92s)]
*  The exchange of letters constituting the provisional agreement between UNRWA and Israel of 14 June 1967, known as the Kamei-Michelmore Agreement, explicitly confirmed that the General Convention governs the relationship between Israel and UNRWA. [[03:11:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11509.92s)]
*  However, Israel's obligations towards the United Nations and its agencies do not derive from this bilateral agreement. [[03:12:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11528.92s)]
*  As established in the General Convention, to which Israel is still a party, they exist independently under international law and remain binding, regardless of the recent enactment in the Israeli Knesset of the unlawful piece of legislation aimed at ceasing UNRWA's operation. [[03:12:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11537.92s)]
*  Israel, therefore, cannot invoke the termination of the Kamei-Michelmore Agreement as justification for failing to uphold its obligations under the UN Charter and the General Convention. [[03:12:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11557.92s)]
*  Moreover, any alleged misconduct by UN personnel must be addressed exclusively through the mechanisms established in the General Convention. [[03:12:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11570.92s)]
*  This does not alter Israel's duty to respect the inviolability of UN premises as a principle of fundamental character already underscored by this Court. [[03:13:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11581.92s)]
*  As such, military expediency cannot justify violations of UN privileges and immunities. [[03:13:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11593.92s)]
*  Brazil also underscores that Israel cannot rely on its domestic laws, including recent legislative measures, to evade compliance with its international commitments. [[03:13:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11603.92s)]
*  Article 27 of the Vienna Convention on the Law of the Treaties unequivocally affirms that states cannot invoke their national laws as a justification for failure to perform their international obligations. [[03:13:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11615.92s)]
*  Israel, as a state party to the UN Charter, has a binding legal duty to facilitate UNRWA's work in the occupied Palestinian territory. [[03:13:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11628.92s)]
*  The issue is not merely one of technicalities or bureaucratic maneuvering. [[03:13:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11639.92s)]
*  The lives of millions of Palestinians depend on the provision of humanitarian assistance, and this Court's opinion is crucial in reaffirming Israel's legal obligations toward the United Nations and its agencies. [[03:14:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11645.92s)]
*  Israel's failure to facilitate UNRWA's operations as a means of obstructing humanitarian assistance constitutes a direct violation of its international legal obligations. [[03:14:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11661.92s)]
*  Therefore, Brazil respectfully urges the International Court of Justice to affirm Israel's obligations under international law concerning the privileges and immunities of the United Nations, [[03:14:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11675.92s)]
*  and to demand that Israel cease all measures aimed at restricting the activities of UNRWA in the occupied Palestinian territory. [[03:14:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11688.92s)]
*  Only through full cooperation with the United Nations can Israel comply with its obligations under the UN Charter, the Fourth Geneva Convention, and other binding international legal instruments. [[03:14:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11698.92s)]
*  Distinguished members of the Court, [[03:15:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11714.92s)]
*  In recent weeks, new and severe antecedents of direct attacks by Israel against staff of international organizations and humanitarian aid providers continued to occur. [[03:15:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11716.92s)]
*  On the 30th of March, the bodies of 15 humanitarian workers from the Palestinian Red Crescent, Civil Defense, and UNRWA were discovered in Rafa, buried in a mass grave, having been killed by Israeli forces while participating in rescue operations in the southern Gaza Strip the previous week. [[03:15:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11729.92s)]
*  In April, Israel bombed a building in the Jabalia refugee camp in the northern Gaza Strip, which housed a clinic operated by UNRWA. [[03:15:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11750.92s)]
*  The clinic had been turned into an improvised shelter for Palestinians displaced by the conflict. [[03:16:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11762.92s)]
*  The attack caused at least 19 deaths, including that of nine children. [[03:16:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11768.92s)]
*  Over 51,000 Palestinians have lost their lives in Gaza. [[03:16:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11775.92s)]
*  Hundreds of humanitarian workers, whose work was solely aimed at saving lives or providing some relief to a desperate population, have also been killed. [[03:16:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11780.92s)]
*  It is within this context that the present advisory opinion is framed. [[03:16:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11791.92s)]
*  For the reasons presented above, Brazil reaffirms and respectfully invites the Court to declare that. [[03:16:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11797.92s)]
*  The Court has and should exercise its advisory jurisdiction. [[03:16:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11804.92s)]
*  B. The Palestinian people have the inalienable right to self-determination and to their independent sovereign state, which includes the right to freely establish diplomatic relations and permanent diplomatic missions without external interference. [[03:16:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11811.92s)]
*  C. As the occupying power, Israel must comply with international humanitarian law, including the Hague regulations and the Fourth Geneva Convention. [[03:17:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11828.92s)]
*  Israel is therefore under a non-derogable obligation not only to refrain from impeding or hindering the presence and activities of the United Nations, other international organizations, and third-party states in the occupied Palestinian territory, [[03:17:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11839.92s)]
*  but also to facilitate and enable the immediate, safe, and unhindered delivery of humanitarian assistance at scale, directly to the Palestinian civilian population in the occupied Palestinian territory. [[03:17:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11856.92s)]
*  D. As a member of the United Nations, Israel must fulfill in good faith the obligations assumed by it in accordance with the Charter, including the obligation to give the United Nations and its agencies every assistance and any action it takes in accordance with the Charter. [[03:17:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11872.92s)]
*  E. Israel is under the obligation to respect the privileges and immunities of the United Nations and its agencies in accordance with the Charter and the General Convention on the Privileges and Immunities of the United Nations. [[03:18:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11891.92s)]
*  We are confident that these are the inescapable conclusions that this Court will reach. Thank you. [[03:18:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11906.92s)]
*  I thank the representative of Brazil for his presentation. Before I invite the next delegation to take the floor, the Court will observe a coffee break of 15 minutes. The hearing is suspended. [[03:18:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=11913.92s)]
