*  The sitting is resumed. [[03:37:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13053.92s)]
*  I now invite the next participating delegation, Chile, to address the Court, and I call His Excellency Claudio Toronso to the podium. [[03:37:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13055.92s)]
*  You have the floor, sir. [[03:37:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13066.92s)]
*  Mr. President, members of the Court, it is an honor to appear before you in these advisory proceedings on behalf of the Republic of Chile. [[03:37:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13068.92s)]
*  The question submitted to the Court is urgent, and comes at a time when international law and the relevance of international organizations are as important as they have ever been. [[03:38:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13093.92s)]
*  In Chile's view, an opinion of the Court on this matter is pivotal to affirming and upholding the rule of international law and reinforcing the legitimacy of international norms. [[03:38:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13110.92s)]
*  Chile recognizes that these proceedings are rooted in the context of the complex situation in the occupied Palestinian territories. [[03:38:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13127.92s)]
*  Chile has continuously supported the self-determination of the Palestinian people, advocating for peace and recognizing the right of both states to exist, and the right of the people who inhabit them to live a dignified and safe life. [[03:38:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13139.92s)]
*  In this regard, Chile would like to stress its firm condemnation of all violation of international law by all parties to the conflict, including the attacks conducted by Hamas on 7 October 2023 and the kidnapping of individuals whose immediate and unconditional release Chile demands. [[03:39:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13164.92s)]
*  When it comes to human suffering, each event is a tragedy. [[03:39:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13191.92s)]
*  In this presentation, we will develop three key points. [[03:40:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13200.92s)]
*  First, I will address the jurisdiction of the Court to render an advisory opinion, and in particular, the absence of compelling reasons to decline it. [[03:40:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13205.92s)]
*  Second, I will address the scope of the question presented to the Court by the General Assembly and the applicability of the obligations that have already been noted by most delegations in the written phase of the proceedings. [[03:40:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13218.92s)]
*  And lastly, Mrs. Valeria Chiappini will address the question of privileges and immunities of international organizations. [[03:40:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13236.92s)]
*  Moving to the first point, it is Chile's position that the Court has jurisdiction to give the requested advisory opinion, and that there are no compelling reasons for the Court to refuse to do so. [[03:40:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13248.92s)]
*  Some States have argued in the present proceedings that an advisory opinion would prejudge essential elements relevant to a pending case before this Court, namely the proceedings brought by South Africa against Israel regarding the application of the Genocide Convention. [[03:41:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13267.92s)]
*  Chile recalls that this Court made clear in its interpretation of the peace treaty's advisory opinion that the Court could decline to exercise its advisory jurisdiction in such cases where, and I quote, [[03:41:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13290.92s)]
*  the question put to it was directly related to the main point of a dispute actually pending between two States, so that answering the question would be substantially equivalent to deciding the dispute between the parties. [[03:41:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13305.92s)]
*  As was the case in interpretation of peace treaties, the question put to the Court in the present proceedings does not touch the merits of the aforementioned pending dispute. [[03:42:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13322.92s)]
*  And therefore, I quote, the legal position of the parties to this dispute cannot be in any way compromised by the answers that the Court may give to the question put to it. [[03:42:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13336.92s)]
*  In the pending dispute, South Africa is claiming that Israel is in breach of its obligations under the Genocide Convention. [[03:42:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13351.92s)]
*  Thus, the relevant question for the Court is whether the acts and omissions by Israel complained of by South Africa are genocidal in character and are intended to bring about the destruction of a substantial part of the Palestinian national, racial, and ethnic group. [[03:42:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13361.92s)]
*  On the other hand, the question raised here concerns the obligation of Israel in relation to the presence and activities of the United Nations, including its agencies and bodies, other international organizations, and third States, which, as made clear by the delegations that have preceded me, encompass obligations to Israel. [[03:43:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13385.92s)]
*  These are the issues that arise from several bodies of law, including international humanitarian law, international human rights law, and the privileges and immunities of international organizations. [[03:43:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13415.92s)]
*  Therefore, although the provision of humanitarian assistance is an issue that arose in the case concerning the application of the Genocide Convention in the context of provisional measures, and it's also relevant to the present proceedings, [[03:43:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13430.92s)]
*  Chile submits that it is not a question that directly relates to the Court's dispute of that case. [[03:44:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13447.92s)]
*  Indeed, by answering the question put before it, the Court would not be deciding any aspect of the dispute between the parties in the contentious proceeding, because there are no direct links between the questions raised in the case concerning the application of Genocide Convention and the question put to the Court in the present proceedings. [[03:44:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13457.92s)]
*  Thus, rendering an advisory opinion would not compromise the legal positions of the parties to the dispute nor the fairness of the proceedings. Consequently, there are no compelling reasons for the Court to refuse to render the advisory opinion. [[03:44:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13481.92s)]
*  Mr. President, members of the Court, this leads me to my second point regarding the scope of the question presented to the Court and the applicable rules. [[03:45:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13501.92s)]
*  The Court has had the opportunity to make findings in relation to the situation of the occupied Palestinian territory on two occasions. [[03:45:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13516.92s)]
*  First, on 9 July 2004, in its advisory opinion regarding the legal consequences of the construction of a wall, and second, 20 years later, on 19 July 2024, in its advisory opinion regarding the legal consequences that arise from Israel practices and policies in the OPD. [[03:45:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13528.92s)]
*  In this context, the present proceedings are meant to complement the aforementioned opinions by addressing questions that had not yet been put before the Court and consequently have not been answered. [[03:45:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13555.92s)]
*  In particular, while the previous advisory opinions address the obligations that Israel has in relation to Palestinian people, the present question seeks to identify the obligations that Israel has toward other relevant actors operating in and in relation to the occupied Palestinian territory. [[03:46:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13573.92s)]
*  More specifically, the question refers to the United Nations, including its agencies and bodies, other international organizations and third states. [[03:46:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13596.92s)]
*  The obligations that the Court was requested to identify relate to all international organizations and states operating in and in relation to the OPD. [[03:46:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13607.92s)]
*  However, Chile requests that the Court take note of the grave concern expressed by the General Assembly in the preamble of its resolution 79-232, which informs the present request from advisory opinion in relation to, and I quote, [[03:47:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13621.92s)]
*  Plans and measures, including legislation adopted by Israel to interfere with or obstruct the presence and operation of the United Nations and the United Nations entities and organizations, including the United Nations Relief and Works Agency for Palestine Refugees in the Near East. End of quote. [[03:47:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13643.92s)]
*  As was submitted in our written statement, it is Chile's position that the relevant obligations arise from Israel's dual role as both an occupant power and a member of the United Nations. [[03:47:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13670.92s)]
*  First, in its role as an occupant power, Israel is bound by international humanitarian law, particularly by the law of occupation and international human rights law, where applicable. [[03:48:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13687.92s)]
*  While it's true, as some have argued, that international humanitarian law does not directly focus on interaction between the occupant power and international organization or third state, it does focus on the protection of civilians and the occupied population. [[03:48:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13703.92s)]
*  In that context, it establishes obligations to provide humanitarian relief and basic services to the occupied population. [[03:48:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13724.92s)]
*  Furthermore, the Fourth Geneva Convention, to which Israel is a party, establishes a specific obligation for the occupant power to grant any relief organization all facilities necessary for it to achieve its purpose within the bounds set by military or security considerations. [[03:48:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13736.92s)]
*  Chile notes that under Article 140.2 of the Fourth Geneva Convention, the scope of the activities that may be undertaken by relief organization is quite broad and would certainly encompass the activities of all 13 United Nations entities that maintain an ongoing presence in the OPT, [[03:49:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13763.92s)]
*  as has been identified by the UN Secretariat in the present proceedings. [[03:49:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13789.92s)]
*  As clarified by the International Committee of the Red Cross in its 1958 commentary to Article 30 of the Fourth Geneva Convention, the obligation of the occupant power to grant all facilities to relief organization is not met by merely authorizing them to carry out their work. [[03:49:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13797.92s)]
*  Rather, the occupant power must facilitate and promote their task. [[03:50:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13823.92s)]
*  This means that it must, and I quote, take all necessary steps to allow approved organizations to take rapid and effective action wherever they ask to give assistance. [[03:50:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13830.92s)]
*  End of quote. [[03:50:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13844.92s)]
*  While this obligation is certainly limited by military necessity and security needs, this reservation must be interpreted restrictively and should not be read as carte blanche for completely prohibiting the activities of such organizations, [[03:50:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13846.92s)]
*  especially when they have been given a mandate to address the occupied population of a particular area by the General Assembly. [[03:51:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13866.92s)]
*  Indeed, such limitations must only be imposed in good faith, and I quote, shall not hinder the supply of effective and adequate relief to all protect persons. [[03:51:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13879.92s)]
*  End of quote. [[03:51:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13893.92s)]
*  For these reasons, the occupant power should show moderation in their use of this reservation, applying it only in cases of real necessity in an exceptional and temporary manner. [[03:51:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13894.92s)]
*  These measures can never result in the paralysis of the relief effort, and while they last, the occupant power must make suitable arrangements on behalf of the protected population. [[03:51:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13911.92s)]
*  Turning next to Israel's second role as a UN member state. [[03:52:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13928.92s)]
*  Israel's obligation stems mainly from the UN Charter and the Convention on the Privileges and Immunities of the United Nations. [[03:52:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13937.92s)]
*  For the sake of time, Chile directs the Court's attention to its written submissions for the complete identification of all the relevant obligations that are applicable, [[03:52:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13947.92s)]
*  and would like to highlight here the duty of all UN member states to collaborate with the United Nations enshrined in Article 2, Paragraph 5, and 56 of the UN Charter. [[03:52:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13961.92s)]
*  It is Chile's position that this duty includes all bodies, agencies and subsidiary organs of the United Nations, and involves not only the observance and implementation of the UN policies and decisions, [[03:52:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13978.92s)]
*  but also an obligation to cooperate in good faith with the organizations and abstain from obstructing their mandate. [[03:53:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=13996.92s)]
*  Your Excellencies, while this duty certainly applies in relation to binding Security Council decisions, contrary to what has been argued by some participants in the present proceedings, [[03:53:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14007.92s)]
*  Chile submits that this duty does not exclusively apply to action taken by the Security Council in accordance to Chapter 7. [[03:53:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14021.92s)]
*  Indeed, this Court has contradicted such narrow conception of the duty to collaborate in two ways. [[03:53:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14031.92s)]
*  First, this Court made clear that the Security Council can make binding decisions in exercise of any of its powers, not only those concerning enforcement actions under Chapter 7. [[03:53:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14038.92s)]
*  Second, this Court affirmed that, and I quote, [[03:54:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14056.92s)]
*  "...the effective working of the organization, the accomplishment of its task, and the independence and effectiveness of the work of its agents," end of quote, [[03:54:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14060.92s)]
*  "...requires the strict observance of the duty to cooperate under Article 2.5 of the UN Charter." [[03:54:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14071.92s)]
*  Further, considering that the obligations contained in Article 2.5 is one of the principles of the organization under which Member States must act in order to achieve the purpose of the United Nations, [[03:54:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14082.92s)]
*  it follows that this duty of cooperation applies to activities of the organization and all its organs and agencies. [[03:54:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14097.92s)]
*  A more restrictive interpretation would render this provision meaningless by limiting the scope of the principles of the Charter only to Article 25. [[03:55:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14108.92s)]
*  Nevertheless, even if the Court were to find that Article 2.5 only refers to Security Council decisions, [[03:55:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14121.92s)]
*  it still admits that the Security Council has decided to vest Israel with specific obligations to allow, facilitate, and enable the safe and unhindered delivery of humanitarian assistance in the OPT, [[03:55:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14129.92s)]
*  and to, I quote, "...ensure the safety and security of United Nations and associated personnel, those of its specialized agencies, and all other personnel engaged in humanitarian relief activities consistent with international humanitarian law, with predileges to the freedoms of movement and access." [[03:55:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14146.92s)]
*  End of quote. [[03:56:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14175.92s)]
*  Mr. President, with this I conclude the first part of Chile's presentation, and I kindly request that you give the floor to Mrs. Chiappini to address our last key point. [[03:56:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14179.92s)]
*  I thank Mr. Troncosso. I now give the floor to Ms. Valeria Chiappini. You have the floor, Madam. [[03:56:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14197.92s)]
*  Mr. President, Members of the Court, It is an honor to appear before you on behalf of the Republic of Chile. [[03:56:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14211.92s)]
*  In the remaining time, I will address the general obligation of all UN member states to accord to the United Nations such privileges and immunities as are necessary for the fulfillment of its purposes under Article 105 of the UN Charter. [[03:56:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14219.92s)]
*  This obligation is further detailed in the Convention on the Privileges and Immunities of the United Nations, which I will herein refer to as the General Convention. [[03:57:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14236.92s)]
*  This obligation is brought in scope and applies to all principal and subsidiary organs of the United Nations, whether or not Member States have entered into any further agreement specifying them, or even if they have terminated such agreements. [[03:57:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14249.92s)]
*  Concerning this obligation, Chile would like to emphasize that Member States have a duty to guarantee immunity of jurisdiction and execution for the United Nations and its staff, and the inviolability of its premises, archives, and documents in a similar manner as those granted to diplomatic missions. [[03:57:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14266.92s)]
*  To put it differently, these privileges and immunities are not subject to any qualification whatsoever. [[03:58:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14290.92s)]
*  Nevertheless, some participants in the present proceedings have argued that these obligations would not be applicable where legitimate security concerns of a Member State are undermined by an abuse of the agency's privileges and immunities. [[03:58:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14299.92s)]
*  This, however, is not correct. [[03:58:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14315.92s)]
*  The object and purpose of these privileges and immunities is to ensure the independence of the organization and to guarantee that it carries out its mandate without any undue interference or financial gain by the host state. [[03:58:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14319.92s)]
*  Indeed, these privileges and immunities are only limited by that which is necessary for the organization's proper functioning. [[03:58:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14336.92s)]
*  In short, United Nations Member States are bound to accord the privileges and immunities that are necessary for the organization to perform their functions independently, effectively, and impartially. [[03:59:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14345.92s)]
*  In this regard, while Chile condemns any abuse of these privileges and immunities that may occur, Chile recalls that Member States are not allowed to take unilateral action against the privileges and immunities of the organization, its bodies, agencies, and staff in the presence of a perceived abuse. [[03:59:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14362.92s)]
*  A specific provision to this effect was included in the Convention on the Privileges and Immunities of the Specialized Agencies adopted one year after the General Convention. [[03:59:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14386.92s)]
*  Section 24 of the Convention of the Specialized Agencies provides a mechanism for state parties to resolve a situation in which they consider there has been an abuse of a privilege or immunity, [[03:59:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14397.92s)]
*  mandating them to engage in consultations with the concerned agency. [[04:00:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14411.92s)]
*  If such consultations fail, it is this very court who needs to determine, through an advisory opinion, whether such an abuse has occurred before any measure can be taken by the host state. [[04:00:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14417.92s)]
*  The original proposal of Subcommittee 1 of the Sixth Committee of the General Assembly was granting state parties to that Convention, in the event of such an abuse, the right to denounce it and terminate any obligation to give privileges and immunities to the specialized agencies of which it would still remain a member. [[04:00:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14433.92s)]
*  However, that proposal was met with several objections, including, first, that if such a provision were to be incorporated, the Specialized Agencies Convention would diverge considerably from the General Convention, which does not grant such right of denunciation. [[04:00:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14456.92s)]
*  Second, the provision would contradict the already accepted principle that specialized agencies should receive appropriate privileges and immunities as necessary to carry out their mandate. [[04:01:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14477.92s)]
*  And third, it seemed wrong in principle to permit a state to have the advantages of being a member of a specialized agency while denying it privileges and immunities necessary for its operations. [[04:01:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14491.92s)]
*  To be sure, Your Excellencies, while there is no similar provision contained in the General Convention, the same considerations still stand. [[04:01:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14506.92s)]
*  Namely, permitting a member state to unilaterally strip the organization and its officials of their necessary privileges and immunities would defeat their very object and purpose. [[04:01:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14516.92s)]
*  Indeed, in the United States diplomatic and consular staff Interan case, the Court affirmed the fundamental character of the principle of inviolability, and consequently found that the conduct of Iran would have been unjustified even if the alleged criminal activities of the United States had been established. [[04:02:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14530.92s)]
*  Mainly because the Vienna Conventions on Diplomatic and Consular Relations contained express provisions to address the abuse of privileges and immunities. [[04:02:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14553.92s)]
*  Similarly, the General Convention offers sufficient assurances against the abuse of privileges and immunities. [[04:02:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14564.92s)]
*  Sections 20 and 23 clearly establish, and I quote, that privileges and immunities are granted to officials and experts in the interest of the United Nations and not for the personal benefit of the individuals themselves, end of quote. [[04:02:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14573.92s)]
*  And provide the Secretary General with the right and duty to waive the immunity of any official or expert in mission where such immunity would impede the course of justice. [[04:03:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14590.92s)]
*  In addition, Section 21 of the General Convention provides an obligation to the United Nations, and I quote, to cooperate at all times with the appropriate authorities of members to facilitate the proper administration of justice, secure the observance of police regulations, and prevent the occurrence of any abuse in connection with the privileges, immunities, and facilities, end of quote. [[04:03:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14602.92s)]
*  Mr. President, members of the Court, Chile further recalls that under international law, measures of self-help are strictly limited to measures of retortion, countermeasures, and self-defense, and where tolerated are always deemed a measure of last resort. [[04:03:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14633.92s)]
*  In this regard, it is a well-established rule of international law that countermeasures cannot be exercised against privileges and immunities of any kind, including the inviolability of organs or agents of an international organization and of its premises, archives, and documents. [[04:04:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14654.92s)]
*  Lastly, Chile notes, as explained by the UN Secretariat, that any concerns regarding the abuse of privileges and immunities of the organization must be properly brought to its attention to be considered in the context of its legal framework. [[04:04:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14677.92s)]
*  In this connection, Chile stresses the importance that the relevant UN organs, including the General Assembly, strengthen its control over its agencies and subsidiary organs. [[04:04:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14697.92s)]
*  If, however, after the appropriate intervention of the relevant organs, any issue remains unresolved, the proper dispute resolution mechanism is already established in Section 30 of the General Convention. [[04:05:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14710.92s)]
*  Your Excellencies, The regime of privileges and immunities of international organizations is indispensable for the independent and effective functioning of all UN organs, including this very Court. [[04:05:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14728.92s)]
*  The erosion of these norms through unilateral action not only undermines legal certainty, but jeopardizes the very fabric of multilateral cooperation upon which the international order rests. [[04:05:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14745.92s)]
*  Mr. President, Members of the Court, this concludes Chile's presentation. Thank you for your kind attention. [[04:06:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14761.92s)]
*  Mr. President, members of the Court, I now invite the next participating delegation, Spain, to address the Court. [[04:06:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14774.92s)]
*  I call upon Her Excellency Ambassador Consuelo Bermanea to take the floor. Madam, you have the floor. [[04:06:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14783.92s)]
*  Mr. President, distinguished members of the Court, it is an honor to address this Court on behalf of the Kingdom of Spain. [[04:06:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14791.92s)]
*  Spain is participating in these advisory proceedings in order to cooperate with the International Court of Justice in the exercise of its advisory powers. [[04:06:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14809.92s)]
*  Spain's oral statement will follow the same structure as the written observations submitted on February. [[04:07:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14823.92s)]
*  It will, therefore, make a distinction between Israel's obligations regarding the presence of activities of the United Nations, other international organizations, and third states in the occupied Palestinian territory, and with respect to that territory, as a member state of the United Nations on the one hand, and as an occupying power on the other. [[04:07:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14829.92s)]
*  This distinction is to some extent a formal one, made for illustrative purposes, since the legal questions raised are inextricably intertwined. [[04:07:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14854.92s)]
*  However, this formal distinction, which is a direct response to the question asked by the General Assembly, is useful in this context, as it calls for the obligations at stake of the member states of the UN nations pursuant to the Charter of the United Nations and to international law to be considered separately. [[04:07:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14866.92s)]
*  Certainly, the obligations to be examined are comprised in the following. [[04:08:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14890.92s)]
*  Rules in the Charter of the UN directly tied to the activities of the UN to maintain international peace and security. [[04:08:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14896.92s)]
*  Rules in the Convention on the Privileges and Immunities of the UN Nations of 1946, which form part of a wider body of diplomatic law. [[04:08:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14906.92s)]
*  Rules that determine the extent of the obligations assumed freely and in writing between subjects of international law. [[04:08:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14917.92s)]
*  And rules that refer to the protection of people and their property in the context of armed conflict and periods of crisis, which therefore aim to safeguard human dignity. [[04:08:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14926.92s)]
*  In other words, these rules either regulate vital aspects of international law and require states to act in a certain way in relation to the protection of central legal principles of international law, such as sovereignty, sustaining peace and elementary considerations of humanity. [[04:08:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14939.92s)]
*  Or are of a marked instrumental or procedural nature and aimed to safeguard and facilitate relations between subjects of international law in the form of treaties or immunities, even or especially in crisis situations. [[04:09:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14959.92s)]
*  Because of this, they are rules that go beyond the interest of a single state and presuppose the existence of a world community based on multilateralism and compliance with international law. [[04:09:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14978.92s)]
*  Spain's statement will have the following structure. [[04:09:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14992.92s)]
*  In the first part, I will address Israel's obligations as a member state of the United Nations. [[04:09:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=14996.92s)]
*  In the second part, we will examine Israel's obligations as an occupying power. [[04:10:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15002.92s)]
*  Israel was admitted as a member state of the United Nations under the General Assembly Resolution 273, Roman III, on 11 May 1949. [[04:10:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15009.92s)]
*  As a member state, Israel must respect the independence and autonomy of the United Nations and assist it in carrying out its activities. [[04:10:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15021.92s)]
*  Article 2.5 of the Charter sets out this obligation in general terms. [[04:10:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15031.92s)]
*  All members shall give the United Nations every assistance in any action it takes in accordance with the present Charter. [[04:10:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15038.92s)]
*  This obligation is necessarily linked to the principle of autonomy and independence of the UN, contained in articles 100 and 104 of the Charter, [[04:10:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15047.92s)]
*  which is a logical consequence of the recognition of international legal personality of the United Nations. [[04:10:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15059.92s)]
*  In accordance with this principle of autonomy and independence, the United Nations is responsible for [[04:11:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15067.92s)]
*  1. determining the matters that fail within its mandate [[04:11:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15074.92s)]
*  2. selecting the most appropriate means of addressing those matters [[04:11:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15079.92s)]
*  and 3. if appropriate, establishing the organs, programs and agencies it considers best suited to perform the related functions. [[04:11:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15084.92s)]
*  In exercising these responsibilities, the UN must follow the established procedures. [[04:11:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15094.92s)]
*  Member states which participate in the decision-making process of the organization must cooperate in good faith with the UN. [[04:11:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15101.92s)]
*  Nothing prevents states from exercising their rights as member states of the United Nations [[04:11:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15110.92s)]
*  and calling for amendments to previous decisions adopted by its bodies. [[04:11:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15117.92s)]
*  They may do so with the sole limit of always acting in accordance with the Charter [[04:12:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15122.92s)]
*  and pursuant to the decision-making procedures of the competent bodies, and therefore not by means of an unilateral decision. [[04:12:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15128.92s)]
*  In Resolution 79-81, Peaceful Settlement of the Question of Palestine, which was adopted on 3 December 2024, [[04:12:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15138.92s)]
*  the General Assembly reaffirmed the permanent responsibility of the United Nations with regard to the question of Palestine, [[04:12:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15152.92s)]
*  until it is resolved, in all aspects in accordance with international law and relevant resolutions. [[04:12:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15161.92s)]
*  Said responsibility was assumed by the United Nations early in its existence. [[04:12:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15168.92s)]
*  The duty of member states of the United Nations to assist the organization, which we have described in general terms, [[04:12:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15177.92s)]
*  crystallizes here as two obligations. [[04:13:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15186.92s)]
*  The first, to cooperate in good faith with the agencies and bodies of the UN, including UNRWA, [[04:13:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15191.92s)]
*  and the second, to not prevent them from carrying out their activities. [[04:13:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15199.92s)]
*  In this context, we must highlight the central role that the UN has attributed to UNRWA, [[04:13:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15205.92s)]
*  which was created by virtue of General Assembly Resolution 302, Roman IV, on 8 December 1949, [[04:13:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15211.92s)]
*  on assistance to Palestine refugees, whose mandate has been continuously renewed to date. [[04:13:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15221.92s)]
*  This mandate was established by the General Assembly in accordance with applicable procedure, [[04:13:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15228.92s)]
*  and may only be modified by the General Assembly. [[04:13:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15234.92s)]
*  No State may unilaterally change or cancel it. [[04:13:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15238.92s)]
*  As a member state of the UN and a State Party to the Convention of 1946, [[04:14:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15244.92s)]
*  Israel is not only required to respect the privileges and immunities of the United Nations agencies, funds and programs, [[04:14:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15250.92s)]
*  especially UNRWA, both in the U.P.-occupied Palestinian territory and in Israel, [[04:14:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15258.92s)]
*  but also to abstain from carrying out any executive, administrative, judicial or legislative action that curtail, [[04:14:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15264.92s)]
*  prevents or impedes the effective enjoyment of the privileges and immunities accorded to the United Nations and its staff. [[04:14:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15273.92s)]
*  The extent and content of these privileges and immunities should be understood in functional terms. [[04:14:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15282.92s)]
*  This functional nature does not empower States to unilaterally determine the extent of the recognized privileges and immunities of the organization, [[04:14:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15291.92s)]
*  or to apply the Convention to a specific situation, or to unilaterally decide which organs, programs and agencies are protected by the Convention, [[04:15:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15302.92s)]
*  or to decide who falls within the categories of officials or experts on missions. [[04:15:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15313.92s)]
*  Lastly, this functional nature does not authorize States to assess the conduct of staff and agents in the performance of their mandates. [[04:15:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15320.92s)]
*  These functions are primarily competences of the Secretary General. [[04:15:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15331.92s)]
*  This was established by the Court in paragraph 33 of its advisory opinion on difference relating to immunity from legal process of a special rapporteur on the Commission on Human Rights. [[04:15:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15335.92s)]
*  On the other hand, the Convention includes a number of measures to guarantee good faith and mutual trust between the organization and its Member States. [[04:15:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15350.92s)]
*  For instance, the right and the duty recognized to the Secretary General in Article 5, Section 20 and Article 6, Section 23, [[04:16:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15360.92s)]
*  2, waive the immunity of any official or expert in any case where, in his opinion, the immunity would impede the cause of justice and it can be waived without prejudice to the interests of the United Nations. [[04:16:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15371.92s)]
*  And the obligation of the United Nations to cooperate with the authorities of Member States to ensure the law is followed as set out on Article 5, Section 21. [[04:16:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15386.92s)]
*  Similarly, Article 8, Sections 29 and 30 establish a system for settlement of any disputes that may arise between the organization and the Member States regarding application of the privileges and immunities. [[04:16:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15398.92s)]
*  These mechanisms allow State parties to protect their legitimate interests and rights and to call attention to alleged non-fulfillment of mandates by organs, agencies and officials of the United Nations, and even to advise of potential abuse of privileges and immunities. [[04:16:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15414.92s)]
*  However, the mechanisms do not enable States to unilaterally judge the actions of the organs, agencies and officials or to unilaterally deprive them of their recognized privileges and immunities. [[04:17:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15433.92s)]
*  Either of these actions would go against obligations incumbent upon States. [[04:17:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15450.92s)]
*  Mr. President, I will now set forth Spain's position regarding Israel's obligation with respect to the subjects of public international law deriving from its status as an occupying power. [[04:17:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15456.92s)]
*  We will examine Israel's obligation under the international law of occupation. [[04:17:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15472.92s)]
*  These obligations, which are part of relevant international treaties and customary international law, have been already referred by the International Court of Justice in its advisory opinions of 2004 and 2024. [[04:17:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15479.92s)]
*  These obligations are a. As the occupying power, Israel has no sovereignty over the occupied Palestinian territory and is legally obliged to refrain from exercising any acts of sovereignty. [[04:18:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15500.92s)]
*  The enactment of the cessation laws and any measures taken by Israel in the occupied Palestinian territory on the basis of those laws and other applicable Israeli legislation appear to constitute an exercise of sovereign powers and are, therefore, inconsistent with Israel's obligations under international law. [[04:18:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15518.92s)]
*  b. Israel has the obligation to administer the occupied Palestinian territory for the benefit of the local population. [[04:19:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15543.92s)]
*  In its advisory opinion of 19 July 2024, the Court affirms that by virtue of its status as an occupying power, a State assumes a set of powers and duties with respect to the territory over which it exercises effective control. [[04:19:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15553.92s)]
*  In this context, the occupying power bears a duty to administer the territory for the benefit of the local population. [[04:19:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15573.92s)]
*  The nature and scope of these powers and duties are always premised on the same assumption, that occupation is a temporary situation to respond to military necessity and it cannot transfer title of sovereignty to the occupying power. [[04:19:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15582.92s)]
*  While Article 43 of the Hague Regulation does not, as such, specify the means by which the occupying power is required to fulfil this general duty, other, more specific rules of international humanitarian law give effect to this obligation. [[04:20:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15600.92s)]
*  c. Israel has the obligation to ensure that the local population's basic needs are met. [[04:20:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15618.92s)]
*  Paragraph 1 of Article 55 of the Fourth Geneva Convention imposes on the occupying power the obligation to meet the basic needs of the population. [[04:20:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15627.92s)]
*  To the fullest extent of the means available to it, the occupying power has the duty of ensuring the food and medical supplies of the population, issued in particular if the resources of the occupied territory are inadequate. [[04:20:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15638.92s)]
*  Paragraph 1 of Article 69 of the Protocol, additional to the Geneva Convention, complements and expands on the concept of basic needs, stating, [[04:20:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15656.92s)]
*  In addition to the duties specified in Article 55 of the Fourth Convention concerning food and medical supplies, the occupying power shall, to the fullest extent of the means available to it and without any adverse distinction, [[04:21:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15669.92s)]
*  also ensure the provisions of clothing, bedding, means of shelter, other supplies essential to the survival of the civilian population of the occupied territory, and objects necessary for religious worship. [[04:21:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15686.92s)]
*  d. Israel has the obligation to accept or allow the provisions of humanitarian assistance to the civilian population. [[04:21:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15701.92s)]
*  Article 59 of the Fourth Geneva Convention imposes on the occupying power the obligation not only to agree, but also to facilitate the necessary relief schemes undertaken by other states or by impartial humanitarian organizations. [[04:21:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15710.92s)]
*  This obligation is recalled by the Court in the order of 26 January 2024, indicating provisional measures in which it affirms that Israel must take immediate and effective measures to enable the provision of urgently needed basic services and humanitarian assistance. [[04:22:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15729.92s)]
*  Moreover, international humanitarian law places limitations on a state's discretion to withhold consent in situations of occupation. [[04:22:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15751.92s)]
*  In case of necessity, the occupying power must agree to humanitarian assistance from other states or from international organizations. [[04:22:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15762.92s)]
*  e. Israel has the obligation to cooperate with the United Nations, international organizations, other states and local authorities. [[04:22:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15772.92s)]
*  The International Court of Justice reaffirmed this obligation in the specific case of Israel in its order of 28 March 2024, indicating provisional measures in the application of the Convention on the Prevention and Punishment of the Crime of Genocide in the Gaza Strip, [[04:23:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15783.92s)]
*  where the Court stated that Israel shall take the necessary and effective measures to ensure, without delay, in full cooperation with the United Nations, the unhindered provision at scale by all concerns of urgently needed basic services and humanitarian assistance, [[04:23:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15804.92s)]
*  including food, water, electricity, fuel, shelter, clothing, hygiene and sanitation requirements, as well as medical supplies and medical care to Palestinians throughout Gaza, [[04:23:44](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15824.92s)]
*  including by increasing the capacity and number of land crossing points and maintaining them open for as long as necessary. [[04:23:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15838.92s)]
*  Even if the fulfillment of the obligation to facilitate the provisions of humanitarian assistance is subject to limitations for reasons of security, [[04:24:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15847.92s)]
*  this right of objection must be interpreted in the light of the principles of proportionality and humanity. [[04:24:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15859.92s)]
*  In addition, said right of objection must be interpreted in accordance with Article 47 of the Fourth Geneva Convention, [[04:24:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15868.92s)]
*  which establishes that protected persons who are in occupied territory shall not be deprived, in any case or in any manner whatsoever, [[04:24:38](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15878.92s)]
*  of the benefits of the present Convention by any change introduced as a result of occupation of a territory into the institution. [[04:24:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15889.92s)]
*  Lastly, we must examine the withdrawal by the occupying power of consent to the presence and activities of humanitarian organizations and other States. [[04:25:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15904.92s)]
*  The law of cessation of UNRWA activities adopted by the Kessenets unilaterally provided for the termination of the agreement constituted in the exchange of letters between Israel and UNRWA on 14 June 1967. [[04:25:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15917.92s)]
*  Pursuant to international law, Israel does not have the right to unilaterally revoke the agreement with UNRWA, constituted by means of the aforementioned exchange of letters. [[04:25:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15937.92s)]
*  Moreover, the general principle of the consent of States must not be considered in isolation, [[04:25:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15950.92s)]
*  but in conjunction with other international obligations to which the State of Israel is subject. [[04:25:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15957.92s)]
*  The obligations of an occupying power are relevant in determining whether a refusal or withdrawal of consent is in compliance with an occupying power's obligations under international law. [[04:26:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15965.92s)]
*  In this regard, such termination must not only be in accordance with the laws of treaties, but also with international humanitarian law, international human rights law and the right to self-determination. [[04:26:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15980.92s)]
*  Israel's obligations concerning the presence and activities of the United Nations agencies, including UNRWA, draw their original legal basis from all the aforementioned conventions and obligations under the international law. [[04:26:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=15995.92s)]
*  Mr. President, distinguished members of the Court, I shall now conclude by summarizing Spain's position regarding the questions put to the Court in a context in which the Secretary-General of the United Nations recalled on 14 April [[04:26:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16011.92s)]
*  that under international humanitarian law, in the whole or part of the population of an occupied territory is inadequately supplied, the occupying power shall agree to relief schemes on behalf of the said population and shall facilitate them by all the means at its disposal. [[04:27:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16029.92s)]
*  The Secretary-General also recalled that under international humanitarian law, wounded and sick medical personnel and medical facilities, including hospitals, must be respected and protected. [[04:27:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16052.92s)]
*  Article 2, paragraph 5 of the Charter of the United Nations provides that all members shall give the United Nations every assistance in any action it takes in accordance with the present Charter. [[04:27:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16068.92s)]
*  In Resolution 79-81, the General Assembly reaffirmed the permanent responsibility of the United Nations with regard to the question of Palestine. [[04:28:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16083.92s)]
*  It was in the context of such responsibility that UNRWA was created, with a clearly humanitarian and development-related mandate which has been consistently renewed until the present day and which cannot be unilaterally amended or cancelled by a Member State. [[04:28:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16095.92s)]
*  UNRWA is being prevented from fulfilling its mandate by the laws adopted by the Kessenet on 28 October 2024, which entered into force on 30 January this year. [[04:28:37](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16117.92s)]
*  These laws, and any subsequent measures to implement them, must be considered incompatible with the obligations of Israel to provide assistance to the Agency in the performance of its functions and the fulfilment of its mandate in Palestine. [[04:28:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16132.92s)]
*  Moreover, Israel, as a Member State of the United Nations and as a State Party to the Convention on the Privileges and Immunities of the United Nations of 1946, is obliged to respect the privileges and immunities of the UN as regards to the presence of the agencies, funds and programmes of the United Nations, in particular UNRWA, both in the occupied Palestinian territory and in Israel. [[04:29:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16150.92s)]
*  Certain actions attributable to Israel may be in conflict with the set privileges and immunities. [[04:29:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16180.92s)]
*  Israel has occupied the Palestinian territory since 1967. [[04:29:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16189.92s)]
*  In the words of the Court, by virtue of its status as an occupying power, a State assumes a set of powers and duties with respect to the territory over which exercises effective control. [[04:29:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16195.92s)]
*  The illegality of the occupation does not release Israel from its obligations and responsibilities under international law towards the Palestinian population and towards other States. [[04:30:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16210.92s)]
*  The powers and obligations of Israel with respect to the occupied Palestinian territory are governed by international humanitarian law. [[04:30:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16224.92s)]
*  Articles 50, 55, 56, 59 and 60 of the Fourth Geneva Convention establish Israel's obligations to ensure and facilitate the fulfilment of the basic needs of the local civilian population, as previously stated by the Court. [[04:30:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16235.92s)]
*  In the event that Israel fails to fulfil the aforementioned obligations, Israel has the obligation to accept humanitarian assistance for the civilian population. [[04:30:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16255.92s)]
*  This obligation, provided for in Article 59 of the Fourth Geneva Convention, is well established in general international law. [[04:31:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16268.92s)]
*  Fulfillment of the aforementioned obligations to facilitate humanitarian assistance may indeed be subject to limitations for reasons of security. [[04:31:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16278.92s)]
*  However, this right of objection must be interpreted in the light of the principles of proportionality and humanity. [[04:31:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16291.92s)]
*  Moreover, as assessed by the Court, such reasons do not exist in the present case. [[04:31:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16300.92s)]
*  The laws adopted by the Kessenet in October 2024 constitute an arbitrary withholding of consent to humanitarian organisations, and in particular to UNRWA, to provide humanitarian assistance and therefore a breach of international humanitarian law applicable to all occupying powers. [[04:31:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16308.92s)]
*  In view of the above, it can be concluded that the prevention of the presence and activities of the United Nations, other international organisations and other states in and in relation to the occupied Palestinian territory is a violation of both the norms of international human rights law applicable to Israel and to the right of self-determination. [[04:32:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16331.92s)]
*  Thank you very much for your attention and your interest. [[04:32:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16361.92s)]
*  I thank the representative of Spain for her presentation. [[04:32:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16368.92s)]
*  This concludes this afternoon's sitting. [[04:32:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16373.92s)]
*  The oral proceedings will resume tomorrow at 10am in order for the Court to hear the presentations of the United States of America, the Russian Federation, France, Hungary and Indonesia. [[04:32:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16376.92s)]
*  The sitting is closed. [[04:33:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16394.92s)]
*  Thank you. [[04:33:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16406.92s)]
*  Thank you. [[04:33:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZDGhsCKUXXk&t=16436.92s)]
